Division of Fujian Province and Establishment of Administrative Commissioners

To Establish in Bandit Areas First

(Fuzhou) The provincial government is actively planning to implement the division of Fujian Province and the establishment of administrative inspector commissioners. The counties under each district have been roughly allocated. The commissioners will be selected and appointed by the Xingying (military headquarters), commissioned by the provincial government, and subject to the direction and supervision of the provincial government, while also acting upon the orders of various departments and offices. (1) To assess the administrative, bandit suppression, Baojia (household registration system), and rural cleansing matters of each county at any time. (2) To guide the policy direction of each county. (3) To assess the performance of each county magistrate, with a general assessment every six months, listing the facts and submitting them to the heads of various departments of the provincial government for separate rewards and punishments. (4) If a county magistrate is found to be derelict in their duties, they may be suspended first, and a temporary replacement assigned, while reporting to the provincial government for verification and handling. The above measures will be submitted to the Provincial Party Committee for a decision and are expected to be implemented within this month, starting with the bandit areas nearby, including two districts in northern Fujian and two districts in western Fujian, with locations set in Shaowu, Yong'an, Longyan, and Yunxiao. Japan Actively Expands the Transportation Network in the Northeast,

Connecting Railway Lines and Opening Automobile Roads

Facilitating Military Transportation, Defending Against Russia, and Eliminating Righteous Armies

Changchun Correspondence: In order to defend against Russia, rule the rural areas of the Northeast, and eliminate the Righteous Army, Japan is extending the existing railways in the Northeast, constructing branch lines and light railways, and opening automobile roads in areas where railways cannot be laid. This is all in preparation for Japan's active war transportation. The names and extensions of the railway and automobile road sections are listed as follows:

Extension of the Lahar Route: The South Manchuria Railway Company (Mantetsu) has incorporated the operation of railways in various parts of the Northeast. Tanabe, the Deputy Director of the Mantetsu Construction Bureau, the Director of the Mountain Railway General Engineering Office, and Sato, the Chief of the Engineering Section of the Transportation Supervision Department of the Japanese Kwantung Army, have jointly announced that the Hu-Hai and Qi-Ke lines, which started construction at the end of last winter, the 190-kilometer section between Tai-Hai and Hailun, and the 40-kilometer extension of the Lahar branch line between Lahar and Nehe, as well as the construction of other station buildings, were completed in March of this year.

Korean Jilin Convenience Road: Several Japanese capitalists are planning to build a light railway in eastern Jilin, starting from the Korean border and reaching Shimenzi directly. Tumenzi is located where Jilin borders Soviet Russia, right in the middle of the Chinese Eastern Railway (CER) and Jihui Railway. Construction of this railway began this spring and is scheduled to be completed in July. The route passes through Hunchun, an important town close to the Russian border. The entire line is 110 kilometers long and requires a total of 250,000 Japanese yen.

Railway Construction Plan: Under the command of the Japanese, the Railway General Administration of the Puppet State of Manchukuo is eager to complete its planned railway network to facilitate military transportation in order to intensify preparations for attacking Soviet Russia and suppressing the anti-Japanese Righteous Army. The following is a summary of the road construction plan for this year proposed by the State Railway Construction Office of the Puppet State: Kuantong Road, from Kuandian to Tonghua, 229 kilometers long; Tongji Road, from Tonghua to Ji'an, 94 kilometers long; Kaitong Road, from Kaiyuan to Tongjiangkou, 37 kilometers long; Huanxin Road, from Huanren to Xinbin, 80 kilometers long; Tonglin Road, from Tonghua to Linjiang, 139 kilometers long; Dafeng Road, from Dagushan to Fenghuangcheng, 95 kilometers long; Haigu Road, from Haicheng to Dagushan, 171 kilometers long; Pingxi Road, from Pingquan to Xifengkou, 92 kilometers long; Lingleng Road, from Lingyuan to Lengkou, 165 kilometers long; Chicheng Road, from Chifeng to Chengde, 225 kilometers long. The total length is 1,327 kilometers. Among the above-mentioned roads planned for construction, the section from Dagushan to Fenghuangcheng was started last year and is expected to be completed in June of this year.

Military Automobile Roads: The Japanese are building automobile roads in the Northeast in the name of commercial operations, but in reality, it is in preparation for war transportation. The operating lines that have already started are the Chaoyang-Chifeng line and the temporary operating lines between Dunhua-Hailin and Chifeng-Chengde, which were all implemented last year. Recently, other lines will be built. The following is a list of the routes that have been opened to traffic: (1) Chaoyang-Chifeng; (2) Chifeng-Chengde; (3) Harbin-Tongjiang; (4) Dunhua-Hailin; (5) Shanchengzhen-Tonghua; (6) Xinjing-Fuyu; (7) Nehe-Heihe; (8) Fengtian-Fushun; (9) Xinjing-Jilin; (10) Taonan-Suolun.

2,000 Kilometers of Highways: The Japanese plan to complete 2,000 kilometers of automobile highways in Liaoning and Rehe provinces by the end of April this year. 1,725 kilometers were completed last year, and automobiles have been running since last year. The following are some well-known routes: Liaoyang-Liaozhong, 59 kilometers long; Beishanchengzi-Liuhe, 37 kilometers long; Nanzamum-Xinbin, 88 kilometers long; Qiaotou-Da'anping, 35 kilometers long; Beipiao-Chaoyang, 40 kilometers long; Chaoyang-Lingyuan, 25 kilometers long; Lingyuan-Pingquan, 92 kilometers long; Chengde-Gubeikou, 90 kilometers long; Chaoyang-Chifeng, 164 kilometers long; Zhuanghe-Dagushan, 71 kilometers long; Tieling-Kangping, 82 kilometers long; Kuandian-Changdianhekou, 50 kilometers long; Liaoyang-Lishan, 21 kilometers long; Anshan-Qilingzi, 14 kilometers long; Anshan-Tanggangzi, 12 kilometers long; Andong-Dagushan, 90 kilometers long; Zhuanghe-Chengzituan, 55 kilometers long.

Planned Automobile Road Network: After the automobile section of the Japan Railway General Bureau merged with the Mantetsu automobile section, it actively carried out the so-called Manchukuo automobile network plan. Recently, what can be realized in its plan, such as the route between Harbin and Fujin, has already started transportation. Those that will be opened this year, such as Andong-Chengzituan and Tonghua-Shanchengzhen, require about 100 vehicles. Recently, in addition to adopting transportation on various opened lines, automobile offices have been established in order to realize their ambitions. The following are the routes in the plan: Beipiao-Chengde, 320 kilometers long; Chaoyang-Chifeng, 190 kilometers long (the above have already been opened); Andong-Chengzituan, 236 kilometers long; Changchun-Fuyu, 166 kilometers long; Shenyang-Fushun, 43 kilometers long; Shanchengzhen-Tonghua, 236 kilometers long; Chengde-Chifeng, 237 kilometers long; Harbin-Tongjiang, 616 kilometers long (the above lines were opened in the spring of 1934); Harbin-Bin County, 104 kilometers long; Dunhua-Hailin, 224 kilometers long; Nehe-Daheihe, 280 kilometers long; Lahar-Nehe, 235 kilometers long; Nanzamum-Tonghua, 189 kilometers long; Taonan-Suolun, 220 kilometers long; Qiansuo-Shimenqin, 40 kilometers long; Yingkou-Gaiping, 39 kilometers long; Niuzhuang-Haicheng, 23 kilometers long; Tanggangzi-Liaoyang, 40 kilometers long. The above lines are being rapidly implemented and are expected to be completed next year, totaling about 3,238 kilometers. This automobile network occupies an extremely important position in industry, politics, and military affairs, and it is hoped that the people of the country will pay attention to it. (Northeast News Agency)

Bankruptcy of Rural Economy in the Northeast

Blocking Grain and Stone and Using Bogus Stocks to Buy

Market Price Collapse Makes Farmers Lose More Than They Gain

Harbin Correspondence: Since the September 18th Incident, the four northeastern provinces have fallen one after another. For two years, the people of the Northeast have been subjected to the ravages of the Japanese army. After the emergence of the puppet organization, it outwardly claimed to abolish exorbitant taxes, but in reality, it levied them indiscriminately and without limit. In addition, there were disturbances by bandits and disasters from floods. The rural economy has been completely bankrupt. Last year's harvest was still abundant, and the farmers thought they could get a little warmth and satiety. Unexpectedly, the Japanese manipulated the Northeast economy, implementing a blockade of grain and stone and prohibiting exports. They also imposed heavy taxes on soybeans exported to Japan, a poisonous plan that could not be worse. The various situations are recorded below:

Prohibition of Grain and Stone Exports

Northeast agricultural products have always been in surplus. In order to bankrupt the rural economy and drive farmers out of their homeland, the Japanese prohibited the export of grain and stone, implementing a cheap grain poison plan. The grain earned by the farmers' hard work is not enough for trade, and life will be even more difficult. If all grain and stone are sold at market prices, the proceeds are only one-third of the annual cost. The Japanese took this opportunity to issue stocks and buy them at double the market price, allowing farmers to get one-tenth of the cash and issuing stocks for the remaining amount at double the price, ostensibly to encourage farmers to invest in the construction of the railway around Mantetsu, nominally a people's railway. In this way, the Japanese used bogus stocks to buy up all the grain and stone in the Northeast. Once there are natural disasters or man-made calamities, famine will inevitably be felt, causing all the farmers to leave their homeland in order to achieve their aggressive ambitions.

Taxes on Soybeans Exported to Japan

The Northeast exports 380,000 koku (a unit of measurement) of soybeans to Japan every year, worth 50 million yuan. Japan relies on soybeans for the manufacture of edible oil, soap, grease, and other raw materials. Therefore, soybeans used for oil production are specially exempted from tax. However, each type of vegetable seed that is a raw material for oil production cultivated in Japan is subject to the resistance of soybeans. Recently, in order to encourage vegetable seed cultivation, Japanese agricultural and forestry families will abolish the tax exemption order for soybeans used for oil production in accordance with the regulations of the 14th year of the Taisho period of the tariff revision law and levy half tax as in previous years.

Plummeting Grain Prices

The Northeast economy is now completely in the hands of the Japanese. The grain obtained through the hard work of our farmers is being arbitrarily priced by the Japanese, causing a sharp drop in value to the level of mud and sand. The grain prices of the Harbin banks and current grain merchants are listed below:

Deteriorating Miners' Strike in Tangshan

Miners Hold Marches and Demonstrations

The Labor Dispute Spreads Throughout the War Zone

Tianjin dispatch: The Kailuan Tangshan miners' strike, after Tao Shangming and Zhao Xun, in conjunction with the local Chamber of Commerce chairman and local gentry, discussed matters with the strike representatives. The workers had divided their proposed twelve demands into two parts: one concerning compensation for the deceased and injured, and the other concerning miners' treatment. Regarding the compensation issue, the demands to the Public Security Bureau were: (1) each of the three workers killed should receive 2,000 Yuan in compensation at once, and the injured should receive 500 Yuan; (2) the platoon leader Cheng of the Public Security Bureau's security team, who opened fire and killed the workers, should be punished; (3) Wang Dexin, the captain of the Public Security Bureau's mining area security team, should be punished. The Public Security Bureau agreed to all of the above conditions. Platoon Leader Cheng was immediately arrested, and Wang Dexin was allowed a grace period. An initial 700 Yuan was allocated for coffin expenses, with the remaining total of 11,000 Yuan to be paid within four days, starting from the 27th. After the workers' successful negotiation with the Public Security Bureau, they turned to the mining company with their demands, including the important conditions: (1) all internal and external workers of the six mines of Kailuan should receive an increase of 8 silver cents on their original wages; (2) an increase in bonuses for external workers, and the company should extract 4 silver cents per ton of coal produced annually and distribute it to the external workers. However, each person should receive at least 15 Yuan per year, and each external worker would tentatively receive 12 Yuan. If they switched to internal work, they should enjoy the same treatment as internal workers. The mining company refused to accept these demands. Tao Shangming and the mediators suggested that the workers make concessions, proposing that the 4 cents per ton was too much, and the annual bonus per person should start from a minimum of 15 Yuan up to 18 Yuan. Using this as a principle, they negotiated with the mining company. The mining company, due to its relationship with the four mines of Majiagou, Zhaogezhuang, Linxi, and Guye, feared that if the conditions of the Tangshan miners were agreed upon, the workers of the four eastern mines would also demand the same. Therefore, they did not agree with the mediators' proposals. The Tangshan Public Security Bureau had agreed to allocate the compensation fees, but the director, Zhao Xun, believed that the police had shot and killed the workers to protect the Kailuan engineers and underground workers, and the fees should be paid by the mining company. However, the mining company believed that this was not the responsibility of the mining bureau itself and refused to allocate the funds. Zhao Xun was quite dissatisfied. On the 29th, the agreed-upon payment date, it was not fulfilled. The workers believed they were being deceived, so at 2 p.m. that afternoon, they gathered over a thousand people and gave speeches in front of the Caishen Temple (Temple of the God of Wealth). Zhao Dazhong, the newly elected chairman of the "War Zone Workers' Autonomous United General Labor Union," gave a very impassioned speech. Then, holding spears, knives, wooden sticks, etc., they marched through the streets, holding demonstrations and shouting various slogans. On the 30th, at 1 p.m., they continued the march, and the slogans they shouted were even clearer than the previous day, such as "(Down with Zhao Xun)," "(Down with the labor union that doesn't reform)," "(Not recognizing the labor union that doesn't reform)," "(Down with the Public Security Bureau chief who doesn't keep his word)," "(Down with Zhao Xun, who lacks sincerity)," "(Down with the mining bureau that doesn't fulfill the 20-year contract and deceives the workers)," "(Support Commissioner Tao)," "(Welcome Mr. Zhao Dazhong)," etc. They still started from the Caishen Temple, passed through Guangdong Street, the Public Security Bureau, West Ma Road, Xinli Street, East Xin Street, and dispersed at Liangshi Street (Grain Market Street). Although the mining company knew that the labor dispute was deteriorating, it wanted to endure the pain for the moment and resolve the issue fundamentally. Therefore, it did not make any overt expressions, intending to wait for the government to suppress the workers and force them to stop their activities and resume work automatically. Tao Shangming, Zhao Xun, and others wanted the mining company to temporarily accept the conditions to quell the labor dispute. There was a slight difference of opinion between the mining bureau and the government, so the unrest continued to expand. On the 30th, the striking workers contacted rickshaw pullers and formed a rickshaw pullers' union, also electing Zhao Dazhong as the chairman. In all counties in the war zone with factories, the Tangshan mine sent workers to instigate action. Workers in factories such as Malanyu and Qinhuangdao all showed signs of unrest. Over a thousand male and female workers at the Tangshan Huaxin Yarn Factory suddenly went on strike on the morning of the 30th, making three demands to the factory: (1) restore the original work procedures; (2) implement the wage increase method every three years; (3) remove the officials who abuse workers. After the workers went on strike, they elected 27 male workers and 7 female workers as maintenance team leaders, and 200 male and female workers as maintenance team members, occupying the factory and changing shifts according to the time. The workers remained at their original work positions but did not work. Zhao Dazhong arrived at the factory that day and gave a speech to the workers, telling them to unite and support the Tangshan miners to achieve their goals. Therefore, the entire city of Tangshan had been tense again since the 30th, and the strike was threatening to spread to the counties in the war zone. (March 30th)

Li Zongren Arrives in Guangdong

Assisting with Southwest Foreign Affairs

Advocating Unified Political Affairs

Guangzhou dispatch: Li Zongren had been away from Guangdong and returned to Guangxi for a long time. Recently, due to important Southwest political matters awaiting resolution, he specially arrived in Guangdong from Guangxi on the 27th of this month to cancel his leave with the Southwest Political Affairs Council and assist in all political affairs. Those who came with Li included Mrs. Li, Guo Dejie, and staff officers Qiu Changwei, Wen Qiaosheng, etc. Those who had previous ties with Li here all went to the Shiweitang Guangzhou-Sanshui Railway Station to welcome him. After Li arrived in Guangdong, he drove to his private residence in Mapenggang to rest briefly. Then, he went to the Political Affairs Council to meet with committee members Chen Jitang, Zou Lu, Lin Yungai, Deng Zheru, and others, and participated in the 113th meeting of the Political Affairs Council that day. Outside sources say that Li's visit to Guangdong this time is to discuss the reform of the provincial system in Guangdong and Guangxi, the selection of future governors of Guangdong and Guangxi, and the establishment of a military branch council in the Southwest. Once decided, Guangdong and Guangxi will have a clear expression. However, Li told people yesterday that he had not mentioned the above issues. Li's main point was that his visit to Guangdong was to assist in Southwest political affairs. It is rumored that the central government intends to abolish the two high-level Southwest agencies, but he has not received official news. He does not know the details of the reform of the provincial system and cannot express his opinion. Hong Kong newspapers have reported news of the establishment of a military branch council in the Southwest, but he has not received confirmed reports either, and does not know the situation. His current opinion on the current situation is to support construction, implement sincere unity, and unite against foreign aggression to save the critical situation. As for the suppression of bandits, it has not yet been decided whether Guangxi Province will increase troops to enter Jiangxi to assist in suppressing the communist bandits. The security situation in Guangxi Province is currently quite peaceful. He recently went to Nanzhai to meet with Wang Jialie, the chairman of Guizhou Province. The discussions were only about developing transportation construction between Guizhou and Guangxi, and did not involve major military and political plans. Furthermore, his recent trip to Vietnam was also of a recreational nature, to help reconcile relations between China and France. Guangxi Province currently focuses on construction and intends to greatly expand its air force, but due to limited financial resources, a complete plan has not yet been realized. Chen Jitang, because Li had been away from Guangdong for a long time, specially held a banquet at his private residence in Meihuacun on the afternoon of the 27th to welcome Li back, and invited party, military, and government officials to accompany him. They only dispersed after 7 p.m. (March 28th)

Songjiang: Villagers Clashing Over Lantern Festival Stopped

Recently, the enthusiasm for lantern festivals among farmers in various towns and villages in Punan has been very strong. The county government and Public Security Bureau have repeatedly received reports and are preparing to issue a ban. Last night (the 1st), several thousand farmers in Tinglin Town suddenly had a large number of iconographic paper lanterns and lion and dragon lanterns, stretching for several miles. The wilderness was illuminated by candlelight, and the townspeople gathered to watch, creating an extremely crowded scene. Yang, of the Second Branch Bureau of the town, fearing that it would lead to trouble, and believing that the lantern festival was a wasteful and useless activity, urgently needed to be banned, specially sent police officers to suppress it. Villagers had a misunderstanding, starting with verbal disagreements, then escalating into mutual clashes, with one echoing another, turning into a confrontational situation. Later, Zhang Baoxiong, the head of the district, came out to persuade them, and the unrest subsided. Zhou Ding, the director of the Public Security Bureau, dispatched Inspector Zhu Song'an to investigate after receiving a telegram from the branch bureau. The extent of damage to the branch bureau's buildings during the villagers' riot has not yet been detailed.

Suzhou: Fisherman and Water Birds Perish Together

Zhang Rongfu, a fisherman from Xiangcheng Township, was 61 years old and usually made a living by using water birds to catch fish. Unexpectedly, all 71 of his water birds suddenly died the other day. Zhang Rongfu suddenly felt unable to make a living and hanged himself to death yesterday (the 2nd) morning.

Fire Kills Two Children

No. 2 Yuecheng along the street of Nantongzimen outside of Suchow's Changmen Gate suddenly caught fire at around 10 a.m. yesterday (the 2nd) after an accident, and was extinguished only after various fire brigades dispatched fire engines to fight the blaze. More than ten houses were destroyed. Yunzhen, an eight-year-old girl from the Fang Dequan household, and Huiyuan, a six-year-old girl from the Zhu Chen household, died, because they were playing upstairs when the fire broke out and could not escape in time. At the time of the fire, Shanghai Fudan University Boy Scouts traveling to Suzhou happened to pass by the area, acted righteously and bravely, and helped fight the fire. Because they heard children calling for help upstairs, they wanted to bravely climb the stairs to rescue them, but the firefighters, fearing danger, prevented them from entering.

Arson by an Enemy Leads to the Tragic Death of Two Girls

The house of Qian Arong in Sunjiaqiao, 3rd Tu, 10th Du, Fengqiao Township, was suddenly set on fire by an enemy at around 9 p.m. on the 1st night. At that time, all eight or nine members of the family were asleep. Qian Arong was awakened from his sleep and saw the raging fire. He immediately fled. He saw someone fleeing with a torch in hand. After the villagers tried to extinguish the fire, the result was that four houses with two sides were reduced to ashes. Xu Qiaodi, Qian Arong's twelve-year-old adopted daughter, and Jinmei, his six-year-old daughter, were unable to escape and tragically died in the fire. The police district in charge has apprehended a suspect, Li Fuquan, the arsonist, and is currently investigating.

Wuxi: The Case of Li Shuyun Takes a Favorable Turn

The case of Liu Zhuomin, the former director of the Second Branch Bureau of the Public Security Bureau of this county, refusing to hand over the seal of office, involving Li Shuyun, the wife of Gu Renfa, the Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, has been reported in detail in this newspaper. The latest news obtained is recorded below:

Summons Issued

Since the county court's prosecutor's office took on the case for investigation, it has telegraphed Gu Renfa to appear in court for questioning. At that time, because Gu had gone to Jiangxi and had not returned, he did not appear in court. Later, it was rumored that the prosecutor's office had issued a second summons. In fact, the second summons was just issued yesterday. The summoned parties are Director Gu and Huang Xutan, the commander of the First District Water Police Junhe Jian. Gu's summons was requested to be forwarded to the provincial government, with the court date being April 4th. Huang's summons was entrusted to the Shanghai Special District Court for delivery, with the court date being April 6th. However, it is widely rumored in the county that Gu Renfa came to Wuxi at 3 p.m. the day before yesterday, and his whereabouts were very secret. After getting off the train, he went straight to the county government to meet with County Magistrate Yan for discussion. Qian Chengjun, the chief prosecutor of the county court, also went to meet him for a long time. He returned to the town that evening. However, inquiries with the authorities did not confirm this statement. However, Pan Songru, a Zhenjiang lawyer hired by Gu, did come to Wuxi yesterday and stayed at Room 46 of the Wuxi Hotel and made contact. Before leaving, he told the accountant of the Wuxi Hotel that if the court had a summons for Director Gu, please collect it on his behalf and forward it.

Suing Gu for Bigamy

Since Lawyer Chao Kun represented Li Shuyun in preparing to sue Gu for bigamy, he has been actively collecting evidence. It has now been found that Gu took a group photo with Ai Chengmei and their children at the Qixin Photo Studio in Hankou on July 17th, 1931. The photo number is 255. Because the time of the photo was after his marriage to Li Shuyun (married to Li Shuyun on June 20th, 1931), the photo is indeed one of the key evidences in this case. Yesterday, a special express letter was sent to the Qixin Photo Studio to request that the negative be kept for evidence. Also, among the evidence submitted by Director Gu, there was a letter from Wu Zonghua, etc., to Gu, in which the content was extremely critical of Li Shuyun. Local newspapers in this county have recorded this matter, but yesterday Wu Zonghua sent a letter to Wuxi to correct the record, denying that he had sent a letter to Gu slandering Li Shuyun. This is indeed a mystery. Li Shuyun's father, Li Zhengcheng, who is currently the head of the cash department of the Hunan Provincial Bank, has heard about this matter and has decided to come to Wuxi in the coming days to seek justice for his daughter.

Evidence Complete

Li Shuyun's defense plea has been drafted and finalized by Lawyers Zhang Shizhao and Chao Kun. The content includes: (1) Gu Renfa should be held responsible for producing Wu Zonghua to court to testify regarding the slanderous letter submitted by Gu Renfa from Wu Zonghua, otherwise he is suspected of forgery; (2) The receipt for 200 Yuan given by Li Shuyun to Huang Xutan, the commander of the Water Police Junhe Jian, was not written by Li herself, but was given by Yi Shouming, a friend of Huang Yi'ou, and this money was not an illegal bribe, because Li came to Shanghai for medical treatment on the 13th of last month and did not bring much money. She sent a letter to Secretary Wan of the Civil Affairs Department to send money to Shanghai. Wan then sent Commander Huang to send 200 Yuan to the residence of Huang Yi'ou, and Yi Shouming issued a receipt, which can be testified by Yi Shouming; (3) Regarding Li Shuyun coming to Wuxi to instigate Liu Zhuomin to resist the handover, Li went to Shanghai for medical treatment on the 13th and has never taken a step beyond Shanghai until she was arrested, which can be testified by Dr. Kong and Committee Member Huang Yi'ou; (4) Gu Renfa admits to misjudging people, and Liu Zhuomin was also appointed by Gu, and is not a private relative of the Li family, so how could Li instruct him to resist the handover; (5) The Civil Affairs Department has a seal supervisor and an examiner, and the seal is in the Civil Affairs Department, not in a private residence, so how could Li Shuyun steal it; (6) Gu's commission of bigamy and fraud is fully evidenced and cannot be denied; (7) Gu's accusation that Shuyun sold offices and collected money should provide solid evidence, otherwise Gu should be held responsible for false accusation; (8) There is also a detailed defense regarding the arrest of Li's mother, requesting that she be acquitted as well. Yesterday morning, Li Shuyun's uncle Li Wenhui and others came to Wuxi from Shanghai to visit Shuyun at the detention center. Shuyun's condition is gradually improving.

Qin Liankui's Remarks

It is widely rumored that Director Gu has hired Lawyers Qin Liankui and Wang Youling as legal advisors, and has contacted Lawyer Zhang Shizhao to seek a reconciliation with Li. According to Lawyer Qin, Gu did hire him, but he did not accept the offer, let alone proceed with reconciliation. Moreover, Gu's position as director is a matter of reporting a subordinate, which is not comparable to a personal lawsuit. Currently, it is the investigation period, and no public prosecution has been filed, so there is no need to appear in court for defense.

Changzhou: Public Security Branch Bureaus Implemented Reduction and Merger

Xu Baoguang, the director of the Wuyi County Public Security Bureau, submitted the plan to reorganize the county's branch bureaus and the reorganization and merger situation to County Magistrate Cai Pei, who personally presented it to Director Gu of the province for inspection and approval. It was considered that the number of police officers, the number of firearms and ammunition, the salaries of police officers, and the location of the establishments all met the standards of the province's reorganization plan for the counties' public security bureau. A special order was given to return to Changzhou to implement the plan. According to the bureau's announcement, four branch bureaus will be established in the city and the four locations of Ximen and Xiaohe and Qishuyan. Ten branch offices will be established in other townships and towns.

Jiangyin: Farmers in Huangshan Port Unearth Antiquities

Zhao Youlang, a farmer in Huangshan Port, discovered three stone slabs that looked like tombstones in a gully on Shajia Mountain on the southern slope of Huangshan the other day. Knowing that there was something unusual, he dug open the stone slabs. Inside was an ancient pit, built with bricks around, which was quite sturdy. The inside was a dark heap, which turned into powder when disturbed. Later, a Korean bottle was found, which was used by Han Xin during his military campaign in the Former Han Dynasty. The bottle contained half a bottle of yellow mud, a bronze mirror, about five inches in diameter, with plum blossoms around it, and the words "Luzhou Zhen Shijia Nian Bazhi Zhaozi" engraved on it. There were also more than twenty Han coins. Unfortunately, the villagers did not recognize them and sold them cheaply to a Tao family nearby.

Haimen: Price Reduction Dispute in Shanghai-Haimen Shipping

The Shanghai-Haimen shipping line originally had five companies: Xinrenhe, Jufeng, Dada, Pingan, and Daxing. In recent years, due to poor business, Jufeng Company's Haimen ship has been sold to others, and Pingan Company's Xinshengda ship has been rerouted to the Shanghai-Ningbo line. Other companies also find it difficult to maintain operations. However, the Daxing Company's Daxing and Fuxing ships suddenly posted price reduction advertisements the other day to attract customers. When the various companies found out about this, they considered this move to be a suicidal policy for the shipping industry. Therefore, they jointly petitioned the Ministry of Communications, the Maritime Affairs Bureau, and the Shipping Association to find a way to stop it, so as to avoid mutual destruction.

Zhenjiang: Leng Yuqiu and Others Prepare to Establish a National Products Company

Major figures in Shanghai's financial and industrial circles, in view of our country's backward production and economic poverty, the import of foreign goods, increasing year after year, with an annual trade deficit of hundreds of millions to tens of billions of yuan, a huge outflow, which is truly alarming, have jointly organized the China National Products Production and Sales Cooperation Association to jointly develop production and prosper the economy in the spirit of mutual assistance and cooperation. The national product factories participating in the association all supply the China National Products Companies in various places with extremely high-quality goods at low prices, aiming to save the outflow of resources and revitalize the nation, which is a crucial plan to save the country. Wang Shuqing, the manager of the Bank of China in Zhenjiang, and Leng Yuqiu, Yan Huizi, Yang Gongya, and other major figures in the business and academic circles, in order to prosper the market in the provincial capital and develop domestic production, have specially jointly initiated the establishment of the Zhenjiang China National Products Co., Ltd. with the Shanghai National Products Production and Sales Cooperation Association and major national product factories. The share capital is tentatively set at 30,000 yuan, with each share being 20 yuan, so as to encourage enthusiastic patriots to actively participate, in order to practically promote the sales of national products and recover the outflow of resources. It is now said that a considerable amount of capital has been raised, and the preparatory office is located at No. 81 Wangjia Lane. The Bank of China in Zhenjiang has begun to collect payments for shares on its behalf. It is heard that the company's goods are all supplied by national product factories in Shanghai and various provinces, carefully selected excellent and novel goods, and the principle of small profits is adopted, in order to reduce the import of foreign goods. It is heard that people from all walks of life are enthusiastically supporting it, and the company will definitely be established soon, adding luster to the provincial capital of Jiangsu.

Yangzhou: Zhenjiang-Yangzhou Automobile Adds Early Departures

The Zhenjiang-Yangzhou Long-Distance Bus Company, because the days are longer in the spring and the Beijing-Shanghai Railway has changed the timetable and added trains for the convenience of travelers, and because the company has a joint transportation agreement with the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo lines, the departure times should be more carefully coordinated. The company has added an extra trip each day on the routes, to be implemented on April 3rd. The early departures from Yangzhou to Zhenjiang are: (1) 6:30 a.m., (2) 8:00 a.m., (3) 9:40 a.m., (4) 10:40 a.m., (5) 2:00 p.m., (6) 4:40 p.m., (7) 6:40 p.m. The departures from Zhenjiang to Yangzhou will be ten minutes later for each trip.

Jiashan: Three Villages Report Thefts Simultaneously

More than thirty bandits suddenly arrived at the home of Xu Jianguan in Yuanjiaham, outside the North Gate, holding rapid-firing guns. They swarmed into Xu's house, tied up Xu Jianguan, and beat him. They also lit torches and burned Xu Jianguan's legs, forcing him to reveal where he had hidden his silver. They looted 380 silver dollars in cash and countless gold ornaments and valuables. After the incident, they went to the home of Lu Siguan in Hujiaham, Houcun, and wantonly looted. Before leaving, they kidnapped a seven-year-old child. At the same time, at the home of Hua Chunpei in Gutali, south of the township, more than ten bandits arrived and looted cash, clothing, etc., worth about one hundred yuan. The Public Security Bureau reported that these thieves dared to gather accomplices and commit robberies and kidnappings at a place close to the city, which was extremely illegal. It has specially dispatched the director of the branch bureau to go to the countryside for an on-site inspection and ordered a thorough investigation.

The Case of a Judge Insulting a Reporter Escalates

Fan Jiuzhi, the executive member of the Jiashan County Reporter Association and a reporter for the Jiashan Mingbao, was insulted in court by Judge Zhang Peilin while listening to a trial at the county local court on the 31st. He was searched and ordered to leave, causing public outrage among the entire county's reporter association. An emergency meeting was convened that night and three resolutions were reached: (1) It is recommended that the High Court request the establishment of a reporter's seat in the County Local Court; (2) The High Court is requested to severely correct Judge Zhang's insult to reporters; (3) All reporters in Shanghai and Hangzhou unanimously requested forceful assistance.

Hangzhou: National Products Exhibition Opens

The preparation for the Hangzhou National Products Exhibition had been going on for many days. A total of more than 70 manufacturers from Shanghai and Hangzhou participated. The opening ceremony was held at the Yangbatou National Products Market at 1 p.m. yesterday (the 2nd). Xu Shiheng, the representative of the Provincial Party Headquarters, gave a speech. Then, Pang Jufu, a member of the preparatory committee, reported on the preparatory process. Then, Jiang Senyu and other manufacturers' representatives spoke and dispersed. The participating manufacturers had begun operations at 8 a.m. Also, the National Products Movement Promotion Week in the provincial capital opened at the Zhejiang Grand Theatre in the New Market at 10 a.m. on the 2nd. More than 2,000 representatives from various institutions and organizations attended. Xu Shiheng, the representative of the Provincial Party Headquarters, chaired the meeting and reported on the significance of the meeting. Then, Xu Changwei and others spoke and dispersed.

Local News

Wang Jingwei Came to Shanghai Yesterday for Medical Treatment

Met with a Group of Reporters and Released Important Remarks

The Japanese Requesting the Sorting Out of Old Debts Is Indeed the Case

That Night, He Took the Night Train with Zeng Zhongming and Returned to Beijing

Wang Jingwei, the President of the Executive Yuan, took the night train from Beijing at 7:00 a.m. yesterday to seek medical treatment in Shanghai. His wife, Ms. Chen Bijun, and Tieci Zeng Zhongming also came with him. After getting off at Nanxiang, he went straight to his residence on Bushi Road to rest. He then asked Dr. Noel to diagnose his diabetes. At 5:30 p.m., he met with a group of reporters and released important remarks. He took the night train back to Beijing that night. The details are described below:

Came to Shanghai for Medical Treatment

According to Wang, the amount of sugar in his diabetes has suddenly increased recently, so he specially took the time to come to Shanghai to ask Dr. Noel to examine him. After arriving in Shanghai today, he has already been examined by Dr. Noel. This trip is entirely to examine his old illness and has no other task. He intends to return to Beijing immediately.

Loan Inaccurate

According to a dispatch from TASS in this city, a group of international bankers recently came to Shanghai to study a plan for an international loan to China. Wang said that this statement is completely inaccurate. Russia is currently actively carrying out its five-year plan, so where would it have funds to invest? As for the international community, there is no such statement either.

Sorting Out Foreign Debt

Regarding the issue of sorting out foreign debt, when Mr. Song (Ziwen) was Acting President of the Executive Yuan on January 21st of last year, the United States requested us to sort out the Sino-American debt. Later, after the Japanese learned of this news, they asked our ambassador to Japan, Jiang Zuobin, to request the central government to sort out the old debts. Ambassador Jiang immediately telegraphed to report, but the Japanese have not yet proposed specific sorting out conditions and methods, so there is no way to proceed. Furthermore, our country's Ministry of Finance had long established a committee for sorting out domestic and foreign debts and is actively engaged in sorting them out.

Central Diplomacy

The exchange of notes between Japan and the United States this time should reduce the tension between Japan and Russia. Our country currently urgently needs to improve its internal affairs and prepare for the future. As for the diplomatic policy, there has been no change from beginning to end. Committee Member Huang Changgu Yingbai will go south to Jiangxi in the coming days to meet with Committee Member Chiang. It is rumored that Huang's visit this time will bring a plan to resolve the North China issue. Before meeting with Huang, I don't

Panchen Lama's Entry into Tibet

Regarding the Tibetan issue, Britain has already stated that it has no ambition to encroach upon Tibet. As for the Panchen Lama's entry into Tibet, it is another matter. The Panchen Lama has a long history in Tibet. If the Tibetan people welcome the Panchen Lama's return to Tibet, the central government will do its best to assist him in returning. However, neither the central government nor the Panchen Lama intends to use force to escort him back. Mr. Huang Musong's inspection tour to Tibet is expected to take place in mid-April.

Southwest Issues

The issue of abolishing the Southwest Political Affairs Committee and the Southwest Executive Department has been discussed several times recently. However, Mr. Hu Zhantang has expressed opposition to this. Currently, it is still under negotiation. Mr. Hu Zhantang has not yet come to Nanjing. The central government still hopes that Mr. Hu will come to Nanjing as soon as possible. However, the rumor that Mr. Chiang Ting-wen's visit to Guangdong carries the mission of urging Mr. Hu to come to Nanjing is not confirmed.

Gu Renfa Case

The Gu Renfa case has now been accepted by the court. There are two opinions on this matter. One is to sympathize with Gu for reporting the crime of a relative. The other is to express disgust for Gu's bigamy. I will wait for the facts to be investigated before handling it.

Ban Hong Incident

On the Yunnan-Burma border, Xue Fucheng previously drew a yellow line as the boundary. According to this, (Ban Hong) is within the yellow line and is Chinese territory, while (Ban Nong) is outside the yellow line and is Burmese territory. Regarding this dispute, we believe it is in Ban Hong, while the British believe it is in Ban Nong. Therefore, it can only be resolved by both parties sending personnel to survey the boundary line. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has already urged the embassy to handle negotiations in Beijing and sent personnel to Yunnan to assist the local government in surveying the boundary.

Returning to Beijing Tonight

Mr. Wang attended today's Executive Yuan meeting and returned to Beijing on the night train last night with Mr. Zeng Zhongming. Also on the same train were Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi, President of the Judicial Yuan Ju Zheng, etc.

Roger to Arrive in Shanghai on Schedule

Sailing on the same ship as Ballard

Expected to Arrive on April 9th

According to the "Ta Mei Wan Pao," the American Commercial Counselor's Office in Shanghai received a telegram this morning stating that Dr. Roger, the expert sent by the US government to China to investigate the impact of the US Silver Purchase Act on China, is expected to arrive in Shanghai on April 9th. The ship he is traveling on is the "President Hoover." Mr. Ballard, a silver expert, is also on the same ship and will disembark in Japan.

Li Jingcong Returns to Shanghai to Discuss

Merger of Two Airline Offices

According to Central News Agency, Li Jingcong, manager of the Eurasia Aviation Corporation, returned to Shanghai from Peiping yesterday morning. He told reporters that although the Peiping-Shaanxi route has been successfully test-flown, it is planned to open it simultaneously with the Guangdong-Shaanxi route. However, the Guangzhou airport on the Guangdong-Shaanxi route still needs to be negotiated with the Guangdong authorities, so the opening date has not been determined. The Northwest route has been suspended since the riots occurred in Xinjiang Province, and no telegrams of pacification have been received, so there is no timetable for resumption. As for the merger of the offices of the company and the China National Aviation Corporation, it only applies to the offices at various airport stations to save expenses, and there is no intention to merge the head office offices.

Shanghai-Guangdong Flights Shorten Southbound Journey

Scheduled to be Implemented Starting Today

Flight Times Also Changed

The northbound flight on the China National Aviation Corporation's Shanghai-Guangdong route originally flew to Shanghai every Wednesday, Saturday, and Sunday, stopping in Xiamen on the same day and arriving in Shanghai the next day, which was inconvenient for passengers. Therefore, starting today, the flight time will be shortened to arrive on the same day to avoid delays in between, and the flight schedule will be revised. Details are as follows:

Implemented Today

The company has decided to change the northbound flight on the Shanghai-Guangdong route to arrive in Shanghai from Guangdong on the same day. Therefore, the flight schedule has been revised and will be implemented starting today. The southbound flight to Guangdong today will fly according to the new schedule. At the same time, the northbound flight schedule, which originally departed from Guangzhou every Wednesday and Saturday, stayed in Xiamen, and arrived in Shanghai the next day, will be changed to every Thursday and Sunday, flying directly from Guangdong to Shanghai.

Flight Schedule

(Southbound Flight) Shanghai departs at 6:00 AM, Wenzhou departs at 9:20 AM, Fuzhou departs at 11:30 AM, Xiamen departs at 1:30 PM, Shantou departs at 3:10 PM, and arrives in Guangzhou at 5:40 PM. (Northbound Flight) Guangzhou departs at 6:00 AM, Shantou departs at 8:50 AM, Xiamen departs at 10:30 AM, Fuzhou departs at 12:20 PM, Wenzhou departs at 2:15 PM, and arrives in Shanghai at 4:40 PM.

Bring Your Own Food

The person in charge of the company told the reporter of the Huadong News Agency yesterday that according to the company's regulations, passengers on the company's flights are not provided with food along the way. However, some passengers are negligent in this regard, and often do not prepare food when traveling, which causes passengers on long-distance flights to be hungry. Therefore, the company hopes that future passengers will bring their own food to satisfy their hunger.

China National Aviation Corporation, China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, and Taikoo Dockyard to Implement Sea-Air Intermodal Transportation

The Three Companies Started Selling Intermodal Passenger Tickets Yesterday

Procedures Follow Steamship Regulations at Sea and Airplane Regulations in the Air

The China National Aviation Corporation and the state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the British Taikoo Dockyard have signed an agreement to handle sea-air intermodal transportation, which has now been implemented. Details are as follows:

Officially Implemented

After the China National Aviation Corporation, China Merchants Bureau, and Taikoo Company signed nine articles of sea-air intermodal transport contracts, it was stipulated that China National Aviation Corporation, China Merchants Bureau, and Taikoo Company would sell aviation passenger tickets and steamship passenger tickets on behalf of each other, with a commission of 5%, and that the rest of the procedures would follow the steamship company's regulations on ships and the airline's regulations on airplanes. It has been implemented on the first of this month, but the first of the month was a Sunday holiday, so it was officially implemented on Monday yesterday.

Issuance of Passenger Tickets

Since yesterday, all aviation stations on the China National Aviation Corporation's Shanghai-Peiping, Shanghai-Guangdong, and Shanghai-Chengdu trunk lines have been ordered to sell steamship tickets for all lines of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and Taikoo Company. All ports on the shipping lines of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and Taikoo Company, such as the North and South Ocean and Yangtze River lines, have also been ordered to sell aviation passenger tickets for all lines of China National Aviation Corporation. China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has also submitted the contract signed with China National Aviation Corporation and the implementation situation to the Ministry of Communications for verification.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Undertakes Water-Land Intermodal Transport

Implemented First on the Jiaoji Railway

Intermodal Transport Contract with Jinpu Railway Signed by Both Parties

Completion of Pinghan Railway Wharf Scheduled for Next Month

Intermodal Transport on Jinghu, Huhangyong, and Other Railways Under Negotiation

After the state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Intermodal Transport Office of the Ministry of Railways established the outline for handling national cargo water-land intermodal transport, the Longhai Railway was implemented last year, the Jiaoji Railway was implemented the day before yesterday, the Pinghan Railway is scheduled to be implemented next month, the Jinpu Railway contract has been signed, and the Jinghu, Huhangyong railways are underway. According to the details obtained by the reporter of the Xin Sheng News Agency, as follows:

Jiaoji Railway

After Sun Zhenwu, manager of the Qingdao branch of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, returned to Qingdao to negotiate the intermodal transport of water and land on the Jiaoji Railway, Zhou Fengtu, a commissioner of the Intermodal Transport Department, received a telegram from Qingdao the day before yesterday stating that it would be implemented on April 1. All intermodal transport procedures have been completed with the Jiaoji Railway. Consignment notes, cargo receipts, cargo notification letters, delivery point stubs, intermodal cargo reports, and cargo stubs for passengers consigning intermodal cargo have all been printed. As for the intermodal price list, it will be sent to Shanghai immediately. The Intermodal Transport Department of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will receive Jiaoji intermodal cargo from today. As soon as there is intermodal cargo, it will be shipped by轮. However, the cargo loaded on the "Gongping"轮, which departed from Shanghai yesterday, was not intermodal cargo.

Summary of the Contract

The Jiaoji Railway and China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's intermodal transport contract totals twenty-nine articles. A summary is as follows: (1) The intermodal stations, ports, and connecting points are as follows: Jiaoji Railway Jinan, Zhoucun, Zhangdian, Boshan, Xindian, Qingzhou, Weixian, Ershilibu, Fangzi, Hamatun, Gaomi, Jiaoji Lancun, China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Shanghai, Shantou, Hong Kong, Guangzhou. Connecting point: Qingdao Dagang Wharf. (2) Intermodal cargo is divided into two types: full carload and less-than-carload. (3) The carrier is not responsible for compensation for intermodal cargo in any of the following circumstances: 1. Cargo loss due to natural disasters, incidents, and other unexpected events that cannot be resisted by human power; 2. All packages contain items that are easily damaged or injured; 3. All easily damaged items are damaged or broken due to improper packaging; 4. All barrels, bottles, baskets, jars, etc. are not tightly sealed, and the joints are not firm, resulting in leakage or water vapor evaporation, fermentation, and spoilage of goods, resulting in loss, damage, or reduction in value and weight; 5. The natural reduction of the physical quality and weight of all goods; 6. All goods have combustibility, spontaneous combustion, or are easily corrupted and naturally corrupted; 7. All original parts of the goods are damp, resulting in mildew, light pounds, or the goods are subject to rat bites and insect damage; 8. All cargo losses are due to the negligence of the consigner or consignee or the person in charge of the cargo; 9. All cargo merchants fail to properly handle the cargo during self-loading and unloading, resulting in cargo losses; 10. All cargo losses are due to not declaring the facts; 11. All cargo is reduced in price due to special circumstances and delays in the time of vehicles and ships; 12. All cargo losses are due to quarantine or epidemic prevention; 13. All cargo losses are due to detention by customs or tax bureaus; 14. All cargo losses are due to war or mass riots; 15. All cargo losses are due to legal sanctions; 16. The original seal and skin of all goods are intact, and the goods inside are not of the same color or quality, or the nature has changed, as well as incomplete and short; 17. All carload goods that are self-loaded by the consigner on the railway's dedicated turnout, such as the seal added by the consigner is not abnormal, the number of pieces of the goods inside is short, the weight is reduced, and the goods are damaged due to packaging damage; (4) The consigner shall be responsible for the water, fire, and other insurance of intermodal cargo, or the carrier shall handle it on their behalf.

Advance Payment of Customs Duties

The Jiaoji Railway and China Merchants Steam Navigation Company have established a method for advance payment of customs duties for water-land cargo intermodal transport, totaling thirteen articles. A summary is recorded below: (1) The Jiaoji Railway and China Merchants Steam Navigation Company each withdraw 10,000 yuan in cash and deposit it jointly in the Central Bank to open a special account for the advance payment of import and export cargo customs duties, which shall not be transferred for other purposes; (2) If the above-mentioned stored advance tax funds of 20,000 yuan are insufficient to cover the tax amount, the Jiaoji Railway Bureau shall separately handle the import cargo tax funds, and the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company shall separately handle the export cargo tax funds; (3) The Jiaoji Railway is responsible for recovering and returning the tax funds advanced for import cargo within seven days from the date of arrival at the destination station. If there is any accident to the cargo, the Jiaoji Railway is solely responsible for compensating and returning the tax funds as scheduled; (4) The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is responsible for recovering and returning the tax funds advanced for export cargo within seven days from the date of arrival at the destination port. If there is any accident to the cargo, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is solely responsible for compensating and returning the tax funds as scheduled; (5) The advance payment of import and export cargo tax funds shall be limited to seven days from the date of arrival of the cargo. If the repayment is made within three days, no interest will be charged; otherwise, interest will be charged at a monthly rate of one cent per day from the date of advance payment; (6) The advance payment of customs duties is of the nature of a current deposit, and the interest shall be jointly negotiated by the Jiaoji Railway Bureau and the Qingdao China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Branch with the Qingdao Central Bank. After the agreement is reached, they shall notify each other in formal official letters for filing.

Pinghan Railway

The Pinghan Railway and China Merchants Steam Navigation Company handled intermodal transport. Liu Hongsheng, the general manager of the company, sent Zhou Fengtu, a commissioner of the Intermodal Transport Department, to Hankou. According to the outline for intermodal transport between state-owned railways and China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, an intermodal cargo water-land transport contract was signed, and Hankou was designated as the connecting point. Freight rates and all intermodal transport methods have been decided. It was originally scheduled to be implemented on the first of this month. However, because the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's wharf in Hankou is far from the railway, transportation is quite inconvenient. Therefore, it was decided to repair and expand the original Pinghan Railway Bureau's wharf on the river bank that is connected to the railway in order to serve as an intermodal transport wharf. Now that the wharf has been completed, China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has specially prepared a barge to install intermodal transport cargo. As for the date of implementation, it is expected to be implemented in May. After implementation, the original Hankou wharf of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will be used as a non-intermodal transport wharf.

Jinpu Railway

After the Jinpu Railway and China Merchants Steam Navigation Company carried out intermodal transport, a draft intermodal cargo water-land transport contract was drafted. After being reviewed and approved by the Jinpu Railway and China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, China Merchants Steam Navigation Company specially sent a commissioner of the Intermodal Transport Department to Pukou last Thursday, and formally signed the contract with Chen Shungeng, the director of the Traffic Department of the Jinpu Railway, last Friday. It was stipulated that the intermodal delivery point would be Pukou, and all stations along the Jinpu Railway would be added to the intermodal transport. China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is for the ports of Shanghai, Xiamen, Shantou, Hong Kong, Guangdong, and the Yangtze River. Zhou Fengtu returned to Shanghai the day before yesterday, and reported the signing process to General Manager Liu Hongsheng yesterday, and the board of directors reported it to the Ministry of Communications. It is heard that the earliest date for implementation must be in May.

Jinghu and Other Railways

The Jinghu, Huhangyong railways and China Merchants Steam Navigation Company handled water-land cargo intermodal transport. Zheng Maizhao, director of the Traffic Department of the Railway Bureau, contacted Zhou Fengtu, the Intermodal Transport Department of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. The intermodal transport contract has also been drafted and is planned to be signed. However, the progress of the intermodal transport contract was suspended due to the transfer of Director Zheng to the position of Deputy Director of the Beining Railway. However, other railways, such as the Ninglu, Zhengtai Road, Pingsui Road, Daoqing Road, and Xiang'e Road, are conducting intermodal transport with China Merchants Steam Navigation Company separately.

Minister of Justice Luo Wengan asked the government for leave to return to Guangdong to marry his daughter and inspect various judicial organs in the Southwest. Now that the matter is completed, he took a China National Aviation Corporation plane from Guangdong to Shanghai the day before yesterday. Outsiders rarely know about this. After a brief rest in Shanghai, Mr. Luo took the early Jinghu train to Beijing yesterday morning at about 8:00 AM with his secretary and others to cancel his leave. It is heard that the issue of the abolition of the Supreme Court of the Southwest will be realized after Mr. Luo arrives in Beijing and consults on it.

The Ministry of Finance Replied to the Chamber of Commerce

The Government Has Not Reduced the Value of Currency

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce previously heard rumors that the government would depreciate the value of the currency, and was deeply afraid that the rumors would be spread and affect the market. Wang Xiaolai, chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, made a statement declaring that there was no such thing. On the one hand, the Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Finance asking it to clearly express its views in order to reassure the people. It is now known that the Ministry of Finance telegraphed the Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating that the government had no intention of reducing the value of the currency. The incoming and outgoing telegrams are as follows:

Chamber of Commerce Telegram

Minister Kong of the Ministry of Finance, Nanjing, regards the rumors that the government will depreciate the national currency as causing abnormal panic among the people. The Chamber of Commerce has received inquiries from various industries, and it is obvious that speculators are deliberately creating rumors to confuse the audience in an attempt to disrupt the market. I have ordered them to feel at ease in their businesses and not to be alarmed. Since the abolition of taels in our country, the national currency law has just been established. At this time, the national economy is on the verge of bankruptcy, the currency systems of the provinces have not yet been unified, the financial organization is not complete, and the financial foundation is not solid. How can we lightly follow the example of others and cause chaos, so that the whole country, from top to bottom, will not see its benefits, but will first suffer its harm. I know that the government has clear insight and knows the slightest details, and will not lightly change it. However, since there are rumors in the market, and it concerns the overall financial situation, the Chamber of Commerce dares not remain silent, and should ask the government to investigate the source of the rumors and declare it clearly in order to dispel the rumors and reassure the people. I hope for a reply by telegram. The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce bows.

Ministry of Finance Reply Telegram

Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, the telegram has been received. The government has absolutely no intention of reducing the value of the currency. I hope that you will immediately inform all industries not to lightly believe the rumors and frighten themselves. The Ministry of Finance.

Jiangfeng Airplane Crashes in Wenzhou

The Fuselage is Slightly Damaged and Xu Chengqi is Injured

The Naval Department Sends the Chutai Warship to Rescue

According to the Daily News Agency, the Jiangfeng seaplane, manufactured by the Aircraft Manufacturing Department of the Naval Department, was flown to Fuzhou by instructor Xu Chengqi the day before yesterday. Yesterday, it was mistakenly reported that the plane had reached Majiang (according to yesterday's newspaper, the draft was adopted by the Daily News Agency). It is now known that the plane suddenly had a mechanical failure on the way to Wenzhou and landed in Qilizhen. Instructor Xu was injured. The Naval Department heard the news and immediately sent the Chutai warship to rescue. The reporter of the Daily News Agency talked about the situation in detail with Zeng Yijing, director of the Aircraft Department, and is divided into the following sections:

Circumstances of the Accident

According to Zeng, the Jiangfeng airplane departed from the Longhua Seaplane Airport at 9:30 AM the day before yesterday (the first day). At 1:05 PM, it was approaching Wenzhou when the engine suddenly encountered obstacles and could not move forward. Because it was not corrected in time, it was forced to land in Qilizhen near Wenzhou. The fuselage was slightly damaged. Instructor Xu Chengqi was injured due to the violent vibration when the plane crashed. He was immediately sent to Wenzhou Datong Hospital for treatment. Yesterday, two telegrams were received one after another, reporting the cause of the accident. They were both drafted by Xu, which shows that his injuries are not serious. It was also reported by Datong Hospital that Xu's injuries were very minor. There was no damage to his head or feet. However, the ribs were seriously injured and there was a risk of developing pleurisy. He is currently very awake and his fever has subsided. There is no danger to his life.

Sending a Ship to Rescue

When we received the telegram about the Jiangfeng accident, we immediately telegraphed the Naval Department to report it. Minister Chen (Shaokuan) immediately telegraphed the Chutai warship parked in Xiangshan Port to go to the rescue. The ship arrived in Wenzhou yesterday morning (the second day) on an accelerated schedule. There have been no telegrams reporting the detailed situation. It has been decided to send Wang Chonghong, an engineer from this office, by airplane to Wenzhou tomorrow morning (that is, this morning) to see how Xu Chengqi is injured. If it is very critical, another airplane will be sent to pick him up and return him to Shanghai for treatment. Otherwise, he will wait for him to return to Shanghai by the Chutai warship for medical treatment. The damaged Jiangfeng airplane is still in Qilizhen. Several workers were previously sent to prepare for repairs there, and they are now guarding it.

Afghan, Bratov, Arrested

According to the Shen Shi News Agency, Bratov, an Afghan who presides over the organization called the Great Asia Revival League in Japan, was instructed by the Japanese this time to transfer from Guangdong to Hong Kong and secretly come to Shanghai to prepare to recruit a large number of traitors, hooligans, etc. to Dalian to hold the so-called Asia National Congress, using the slogan of the national liberation movement to achieve its purpose of disturbing Chinese society. The local authorities of the Chinese Concession believed that the rogue's arrival in China was a security risk, so they arrested him at 9:00 AM the day before yesterday when a certain 輪 docked at the Nan City Wharf. He is still being detained by the Municipal Public Security Bureau. It is heard that Mr. Bratov did not carry an entry passport when he came to China this time. The Public Security Bureau has asked the Municipal Government for instructions on how to deal with this matter in the future.

We have high hopes for you. Chairman Kong. B. (Abbreviated) The Executive Yuan's instruction No. 1570 was opened and checked. Tianjin Bang Customs Clearance Workers Stage a General Strike Yesterday

Party and Government Agencies Send Personnel to Investigate the Truth

According to the Da Gong News Agency, the customs clearance workers decided to declare a general strike yesterday morning due to the Tianjin Bang customs clearance firms' cancellation of the vehicle force case, which was decided by the general meeting of all members. Party and government agencies sent personnel to investigate the truth. The Customs Clearance Industry Association held an emergency meeting last night to discuss solutions. The various situations are recorded below:

Strike Yesterday Morning

All the Yangbu department workers of the Tianjin Bang customs clearance firms declared a general strike yesterday morning due to their opposition to the cancellation of the vehicle force. The customs clearance firms involved in the strike are: (1) Sanyang Jingqiao Jiqingli Xinglin; (2) Jiangxi Road Guangdong Road Tongchenggong; (3) Yong'an Street Yonganfang Gongtai in the French Concession; (4) Dama Road Xiangxingli Yufengsheng; (5) Yong'an Street Litaichang; (6) Sanyang Jingqiao Taichangxiang, etc., totaling more than 180 workers. All the Tianjin cotton cloth exported yesterday on the Taikoo Company's Luzhou輪 and Dalian Company's Yijin丸 was completely stored in the warehouse.

Grouped Inspection

After the Tianjin Bang workers declared a strike, they also appointed an inspection team of 64 people, divided into ten groups, to conduct inspections at various wharves, shipping companies, and factories. The groups are: the first group, various shipping companies, the Bund New Customs Wharf, Datong Wharf; the second group, Japanese-owned Nei Wai Mian No. 3 Factory; the third group, Nei Wai Mian No. 5 and No. 6 Factories, and Yitongxing; the fourth group, Japanese-owned Rihua Xihe Yarn Factory, British-owned Public Welfare Yarn Factory, Nei Wai Mian No. 1 Factory; the fifth group, Toyota Shenxin No. 1 Factory; the sixth group, Donghua, Shenxin No. 5 Factory; the seventh group, Japanese-owned Shanghai No. 4 and No. 5 Factories, Shenxin No. 6 Factory, Yongan No. 1 Factory; the eighth group, Shanghai No. 3 Factory, Waitongxing; the ninth group, Japanese-owned Dakang, Yufeng; the tenth group, Shenxin No. 7 Factory, Gongda No. 2 Factory, British-owned Jardine Matheson, and various wharves along the Huangpu River. The order was quite strict.

Party and Government Investigation

Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, the representatives of the Civil Training Section of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Long Peiyun, and the representatives of the three sections of the Social Bureau, Zhu Guilin, went to the Customs Clearance Industry Union in Panjia Lane, Lao Beimen, to investigate the strike situation, and then went to the Customs Clearance Industry Association on Tianzhutang Street to investigate, and urged the association to quickly find a way to stop it and maintain the original vehicle force of the workers to avoid expanding the dispute. Wang Yanling, the executive committee member of the association, accepted the advice of the party and government agencies and held a meeting to discuss solutions.

Bilateral Conference

The Association of Customs Brokers, in order to discuss solutions, specially convened an interim supervisory meeting yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM. Chairman Shi Zhikun reported on the situation, and several solutions were immediately decided and submitted to Party and government organs for processing. The Customs Brokers' Trade Union, on the other hand, decided to hold a general meeting today at 2:00 PM to organize a strike committee responsible for handling strike matters.

Reporting of the Circumstances

A document from the Customs Brokers' Union to the Party and government organs stated: "We are submitting this to report that the Tianjin merchant capitalists are depriving workers of their benefits, only seeking their own enrichment, disregarding the lives of countless workers, daring to act improperly, and wantonly ruining them (above omitted). The origin of the said transportation fee is neither taken from the trade nor from the customers, but is entirely provided by the factory (the factory that produces the goods). The workers take it from the factory, so how can it harm the trade in the slightest? Previously, your association summoned both parties for questioning. The capitalists, knowing they were in the wrong, made excuses, saying that there are many Japanese customs brokers in Tianjin, and their shipping prices are cheaper than those of Chinese merchants. In order to compete for business, they resorted to this measure. Such arguments are even more absurd. Your association saw through their trickery and ordered the Association of Customs Brokers to take responsibility for handling it (middle omitted). Now, for the sake of safeguarding their own livelihood, the workers have passed a resolution in the general meeting to declare a strike until final victory. We earnestly request that you swiftly and severely punish the capitalists who are undermining the vehicle force, so as to relieve the people's suffering and prevent the expansion of disputes. We submit this with utmost urgency, awaiting your orders."

### Shanghai North National Exhibition Decides to Extend for One Week

Scheduled to Close on April 10th

Parade Rally on the 5th

The Shanghai North National Products Exhibition, organized by the Shanghai Chinese National Products Manufacturers Association, was originally scheduled to last for two weeks, opening on the 22nd of last month and closing on the 4th of this month. Whether to extend the exhibition was to be decided by the representatives of the participating factories. The association specially convened a meeting of representatives of participating factories yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM. Details are recorded below.

Factories Present

Yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM, representatives from the following factories attended, including: Limin Dyeing and Weaving Factory, Shanghai Light Bulb Company, Huasheng Electric Manufacturing Factory, Dacheng Weaving Factory, China Products Company, Fuxin Cloth Factory, Hefeng Sock Factory, Xinsheng Underwear Company, Yichang Steel Factory, Family Biscuit Factory, Fengxiang Cotton Weaving Factory, Huasheng Rubber Factory, May 30th Soap Factory, Meifang Cosmetics Factory, Guangdong Brothers Rubber Company, Wuzhou Gubeng Soap Factory, Nanyang Soap and Candle Factory, Lao Shuangcheng Copperware Factory, and more than sixty other factories, with over eighty representatives.

Excerpts from the Agenda

Liu Zhongying was publicly elected as chairman. After the formalities were observed, the chairman reported the purpose of the meeting, and then the discussion began. (1) Regarding whether the exhibition, scheduled to close on April 4th, should be extended, it was resolved that the exhibition period should be extended for one week, closing on April 10th. (2) Regarding whether the association should expand national product promotion during the extension period and hold a parade rally, it was resolved that a parade rally should be held at 9:00 AM on the 5th of this month. Participating factories should send at least two representatives each to attend the parade. Flags and advertisements should be prepared by the factories themselves. (3) Regarding how to raise funds for electricity, meals, and all expenses during the extension period, it was resolved that each booth should pay five yuan and each factory should pay two yuan and fifty cents for entertainment fees. The rest is omitted.

Notice of Extension

After the meeting, the association immediately sent a letter to all factories regarding the extension, stating: "We hereby inform you that, considering the prevalence of foreign goods in the Shanghai North area, and the economic depression since the January 28th Incident, we have specially organized the Shanghai North National Products Exhibition to revitalize the market and promote national products. The exhibition was originally scheduled for two weeks, from March 22nd to April 4th. Now, it has been resolved at the second meeting of representatives on April 2nd to extend the exhibition for one week, until April 10th. We hereby record this and send it to you, hoping you will take note."

Japanese Economic Aggression

What are the Feelings of the Chinese People?

The increase in fares by the river steamer alliance has aroused opposition from the river transport guilds, leading to a halt in cargo handling and creating an opportunity for the smooth sale of Japanese goods upstream. Now, Japanese steamers are going a step further, plotting to resume upriver routes, from Hankou to Shashi and Yichang. The Nisshin Steamship Company has already dispatched the Shinyo Maru to resume navigation. It is currently undergoing major repairs in Shanghai, scheduled to sail for the first time on the 21st. The Japanese are meticulously planning to expand the market for Japanese goods and seize our country's shipping industry. What will the Chinese people's feelings be towards Japanese economic aggression?

According to the Central News Agency, the artifacts from the Palace Museum stored in Shanghai were originally scheduled to be inspected yesterday morning by four representatives designated by the Municipal Party Department, as well as Section Chief Li Dachao of the Municipal Government, and nine inspectors designated by the Shanghai Office of the Palace Museum. However, the Municipal Government believed that the artifacts were numerous and that it was difficult for those without specialized knowledge of antiquities to distinguish their authenticity. Therefore, it was proposed to hire experts in the鑒别 of antiquities to jointly inspect the artifacts with the inspectors designated by various organs, in order to ascertain the authenticity of the artifacts. It is reported that experts in the鑒别 of antiquities are still being sought, so the inspection of the Palace Museum artifacts did not begin yesterday morning.
