Yu Fengzhi Returned to China and Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday

Madam Liu Wendao Arrived Together

According to the Huadong News Agency, Yu Fengzhi, the wife of Zhang Xueliang, went abroad with Zhang last year and began her journey back to China from Europe last month. She was on the Italian ship Conte Rosso, which arrived in port at 2:50 PM yesterday. The ship docked at the Qichang Pier in Pudong. Those who went to greet her included Yang Hu and his wife, the head of the Municipal Security Department, Zhang's American advisor Donald, Tang Shixuan, the secretary of the Municipal Government, and many of Zhang's subordinates. The Municipal Government also sent a public security launch to welcome her. Zhao Erxiaojie and one of Zhang's young sons also came with Madam Zhang. In addition, Madam Liu Wendao, the wife of our country's envoy to Italy, also came. After disembarking, Madam Zhang and others transferred to the public security launch to cross the river to the Jinliyuan Pier at the Sixteenth Concession, where they landed. They will rest in Shanghai for a few days before going to Hankou.

Zhabei Agricultural Exhibition Closed Yesterday

Next Time in Yinxiang District

The agricultural products mobile exhibition organized by the Shanghai Municipal Farmers' Association held its opening ceremony the day before yesterday (the 1st) at the Charity Hall on Liuying Road in Zhabei. Over 10,000 people from all walks of life, including the Municipal Party Department, the Commodity Inspection Bureau, the anti-Japanese Major General Jiang Minsheng, and farmers from various districts, went to visit. The exhibition closed at 7:00 PM last night. The next exhibition is scheduled to be held in Yinxiang District. The situation at the venue is recorded below.

A Glimpse of the Venue

Yesterday was the second day of the exhibition. At the exhibition venue, a pine and cypress arch was erected, with the Party and national flags flying high. There was a white cloth couplet, which read: (Cultivation relies on farmers, hoping for abundant farmland productivity; Improvement relies on science, to preserve varieties for people to view.) At the entrance were Boy Scouts and patrolmen from the Public Security Bureau, standing tall and spirited. Inside was the exhibition hall, which included improved agricultural implements from the Dahua Farm, drawings from the Agricultural College of Central University, and various survey forms from the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau. Thousands of agricultural products, including silk, tea, cotton, beans, rice, millet, wheat, rice, fisheries, animal husbandry, silkworm cocoons, pest specimens, and pesticides, were displayed in separate rooms, in an orderly manner. This shows the dedication of the organizers and their enthusiasm for awakening farmers to improvement.

Raffle Prizes

All members of the Municipal Farmers' Association who attended had previously received over 600 raffle tickets issued by the Municipal Farmers' Association. A lottery was held on the spot, and all winners were given exquisite gifts such as Yonghe Industrial Company toothpaste and balls, Dachang Rubber Factory running shoes and galoshes. A stage was set up in the open space to perform various dramas to entertain the guests.

Gu Village National Products Movement in Baoshan County

The Gu Village National Products Movement in Baoshan County was held on April 1st. The opening ceremony was held at 9:00 AM. After the formalities were observed, Mr. Wang Yiqing, the director of the Gu Village Public Education Center, gave a report, stating that Gu Village's industry and commerce are becoming increasingly developed, and the lives of residents are gradually becoming westernized. It is necessary to remedy this. Therefore, he and local people Gu Zhenyi, Wang Yuming, Gu Jichang, and others organized a preparatory committee for the National Products Movement. Then, County Chief Long Tiyao, Municipal Party Department representative Liu Puzhen, and Education Bureau Chief Feng Maiying gave speeches. Pan Yangyao and Zhao Housheng gave lectures. In the afternoon, a parade was performed, with participants including the public music team, the Zhu Family Martial Arts Troupe, the Dachang Lizhi Society, and elementary schools such as Jujuan Guangfu Gu Village. The association also held an exhibition of native cloth, displaying over 450 varieties. It is said that the native cloth will continue to be exhibited for a week.

Long-Distance Telephone Communication Open on the Danyang-Longtan Section of the Beijing-Shanghai Line

The new land and water lines between Zhenjiang and Yangzhou on the Beijing-Shanghai long-distance telephone line have been connected and have been directly communicating with the Beijing-Shanghai line since April 1st. In addition, long-distance telephones in Danyang and Longtan, two locations on the Beijing-Shanghai line, which were not equipped with telephones, were recently installed and a business office was established, which began operations yesterday. From now on, long-distance telephone calls in the Danyang-Longtan section can be directly connected.

China Ship Insurance Association Opened Yesterday

In order to facilitate business and promote full cooperation among companies in the insurance industry, the China Ship Insurance Association was jointly established by various companies handling ship insurance. The association assumes joint responsibility. The association is located at 160 Avenue Edward VII. Tang Danhua of Huaan Company has been hired as the director. All ships previously insured by various companies have been transferred to the association for handling. All new ship insurance policies will be issued by the association in the future. Yesterday was the opening day. The members include Huaan, Shanghai Lianbao, Zhaotai, Ning Shao, Sincere, Taiping, Liantai, Yongning, China, and Maritime, a total of nine companies. These companies have a long history of handling this type of insurance. Most of the Chinese merchant ships are jointly underwritten by these companies.

The Shanghai-Qingpu Road Will Be Open to Traffic Next Month

The Hongqiao Airport West Side Has Been Completed

The highway from Hongqiao Airport to Qingpu was started in 1929. The route was determined long ago and was scheduled to be completed in 1933. The road passes through Qibao, Beiwujiahang, Xujing, Songzecun, and Qingpu, and reaches Zhujiajiao. The roadbed from the west side of the airport to Songzecun has been completed by the end of last month. It is reported that it will be open to traffic next month. Shanghai cars can directly reach Wujiahang and other places.

Rickshaw Lessees Prepare to Organize the Lianyi Association

Will Submit to Party and Government Organs for Filing

Declare That Lessees Have Heavy Responsibilities and Meager Profits

According to Xin Xin News Agency, rickshaw lessees Yuan Guilin, Zhu Shuangxi, Jiang Fuying, Jin Xinglin, Chen Guigen, and others initiated the organization of the (Rickshaw Lessees Lianyi Association). A preparatory discussion meeting was held yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM. Wang Qile, Shi Changyuan, Wang Zuohong, and fifteen others attended. Yuan Guilin was publicly elected as chairman. The following was discussed: (1) Soliciting members. It was resolved that the preparatory committee should solicit rickshaw lessees to join the association from various rickshaw companies. (2) Submitting to Party and government organs for filing. It was resolved that Yuan and Zhu should be responsible for handling the submission. (3) Announcing the lessee's declaration. It was resolved and passed. The general idea is that the rickshaw problem is not well understood by the outside world, and many people believe that the small bosses profit from it, which is not in line with the facts. It is conceivable that the rickshaw pullers come to Shanghai from the countryside because they are forced by economic problems and the need for food. If each rickshaw puller directly rented a rickshaw from the owner, they would have to pay a deposit of 15 to 30 yuan, pay the rent first, and then obtain a license before they could negotiate. How can the tens of thousands of rickshaw pullers in Shanghai pay this amount? Therefore, we and others, in view of this, lend the appropriate amount and contract for the rickshaws. If a rickshaw puller's daily fare is not enough to pay the rent, and they must fall short, we and others must not be shortchanged by the owner. Otherwise, the owner will immediately withhold the license, preventing us from operating. This is the fundamental problem and the hidden pain of us and others. As for the rickshaw pullers' daily toil, they are barely able to feed themselves. Whether they can find another place to live is also an extremely difficult problem. In order to take care of their lives, we and others not only lease rickshaws on their behalf, but also provide the utensils, stoves, electricity, and tap water they use every day, which is not easy. We ask ourselves whether we can treat the rickshaw pullers fairly. Please think carefully about whether the small bosses are simply reaping the benefits without taking responsibility. To put it bluntly, after paying the rickshaw owners who reap the benefits without taking responsibility, each rickshaw only earns two or three jiao per day. We can only narrow the scope and work hard. Moreover, the cost of living is very high now. Each rickshaw has two shifts, morning and evening, and there are about four or five people who take turns. How can this meager income meet the needs of so many people? It would be impossible without us and others sharing this heavy responsibility with the rickshaw pullers. Also, the inspection fee has always been managed by the rickshaw owners. Last year, due to the changes made by the rickshaw owners, this fee was mostly borne by the small bosses. If a rickshaw puller has an accident on the road, we and others are responsible. Whose harsh rule is this? Therefore, we are publishing this to clarify the situation. If there is even half a word that is false, please conduct an on-site investigation to clarify the truth.

The Two-Roads Administration Rectifies the Wusong Machine Factory and Materials Factory

Both Factory Directors Suspended and Other Personnel Assigned to Take Over

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, since the labor unrest occurred at the Wusong Materials Factory and Machine Factory of the Two-Roads last year and Mo Heng was expelled, there was also the arrest of all the union officers last month. In order to rectify the factory affairs, the Two-Roads Administration has changed the factory directors. Details are recorded below.

Changing the Factory Directors

On March 31st, the bureau ordered the suspension of Mao Erwei, the director of the Wusong Machine Factory, and the transfer of Chen Fuhai, an engineer from the Shanghai-Jiading section of the Machinery Department, to fill the position. Zhang Minjian, the director of the Wusong Materials Factory, was also suspended, and Zhang Yiyan, a clerk from the General Affairs Section of the Materials Department, was appointed to act as the director. The handover was carried out on the same day.

Road Bureau Public Notice

In order to comply with the Ministry of Railways' approved plan to improve the machinery of the road, and actively rectify the Wusong Machine Factory, the Road Bureau has transferred Chen Fuhai, an engineer from the Shanghai-Jiading section of the Machinery Department, to be the director of the factory, and ordered the factory director to implement the following points: (1) From the factory director down, all must strictly obey the orders of superiors and abide by all laws and regulations, in accordance with the organizational system. (2) Protect employees who are diligent in their work and of upright character. (3) Reform working methods and increase production efficiency. (4) During working hours, without justifiable reason, do not leave their own workplace without authorization and break into other departments. (5) Those who falsely ask for leave will be dismissed once verified. (6) Ban those who, in the name of transporting work, do not work themselves and obstruct others from working. (7) If there are gatherings in the factory in the future, regardless of their nature, they must first obtain the factory director's formal written permission. (8) The weekly commemoration of the Premier should be held by the factory director, taking into account the circumstances, and the order should be limited to the provisions of the Premier's Memorial Week Ordinance promulgated by the Central Government. No opportunity should be taken to raise any issues that would undermine the solemnity of the Memorial Week and desecrate the Premier. This notice is to be issued to all workers in the factory for their information, and they must work together under the leadership of the factory director to make the factory affairs progress day by day, which will benefit this road, and we have high hopes for them. This notice, March 31st, 23rd year of the Republic of China.

The Umbrella Industry Labor Unrest is Deadlocked

The Capitalists Decided to Suspend Business from Today

At the Same Time, Petition the Social Affairs Bureau Again

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the strike of workers at 53 umbrella factories including Huali Time has been mediated by Party and government organs. The capitalists held a joint meeting yesterday and decided to announce the suspension of business from today. Details are recorded below.

Mediation in Progress

Since the strike of umbrella industry workers, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau and the Municipal Party Department have sent personnel to investigate the truth and advised the workers to resume work first. They will wait for the Labor-Capital Mediation Committee to be convened in accordance with the law to mediate the labor-capital conditions. Yesterday afternoon, Lu Yinchu of the Municipal Party Department, together with Zhu Guilin of the Social Affairs Bureau, advised the workers and were said to have scheduled a hearing for both labor and capital to facilitate mediation.

Decision to Suspend Business

The umbrella industry factories, including Huali Time, held a joint meeting at 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon. The chairman first reported on the situation of the workers' strike, and then the discussion began. It was decided on the spot that (1) if the workers do not resume work, they will all announce the suspension of business from tomorrow (i.e., today). (2) At the same time, representatives from each factory will be sent to the Social Affairs Bureau to petition again.

The Public Security Bureau and Social Affairs Bureau Prohibit Welcoming Gods and Offering Sacrifices

It was previously rumored that residents of the South City in this city would hold a City God festival on Qingming Day. The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, on the orders of the Municipal Government, stated that welcoming gods and offering sacrifices wastes people's wealth and promotes superstition, which is a prohibited practice. It should be investigated and dealt with according to the case. Yesterday, the two bureaus jointly issued a notice strictly prohibiting it, and the Public Security Bureau ordered its subordinates to prohibit it.

The Widely Reported Case of Exhumation and Re-examination in Chongming Determines That It Was Definitely Suicide

丨Re-examination Results from the Zhenru Forensic Institute丨

Qiu Yinxiang, the daughter of Qiu Chuanlang from Xin Kaihe Town, Chongming, married Yang Miaolang, who lived nearby. Due to discord between the two families, the young couple had a difficult time. After several storms and lawsuits, the young couple were reunited, and their love was crystallized. She was eight months pregnant. However, in May of last year, Qiu Yinxiang suddenly hanged herself. The manner of death was extremely tragic. After her death, Qiu Chuanlang filed a lawsuit with the county government, claiming that his daughter had been injured to death by Yang's mother and sister, and that the suicide was a cover-up. Yang, on the other hand, claimed that his wife's death was due to his father-in-law's insistence on preventing the couple from reuniting. She was held back and beaten, so she took her own life out of resentment. Therefore, his wife's death was actually caused by her father. After the county's examination, it was determined that she had committed suicide by hanging. Qiu Chuanlang was still unwilling and appealed to the Jiangsu High Court. The case was transferred to the jurisdiction of the Shanghai District Court for re-examination and investigation. Prosecutor Yang An summoned both parties and transported the body and coffin to Shanghai, sending them to the Zhenru Forensic Institute for exhumation and examination. As there were no external injuries, internal organs were taken and subjected to a lengthy chemical examination, as well as bone steaming and examination. The chemical examination results from the previous day still showed no injuries and confirmed that she had committed suicide by hanging. Therefore, a diagnosis was prepared and sent to the court. After the prosecutor opened the court and questioned them, they were ordered to leave. Therefore, the widely reported case of exhumation and re-examination in Chongming has come to an end.

A Large Group of Hoodlums Causes a Great Disturbance at the Republic Theater

Where Was Pan Guoliang Taken?

Trouble Arises from Watching a Free Show

The Republic Theater, located at Xiaocai Chang, Gonghe Road, Zhabei, was showing "Fen Zhuang Lou" on stage from 4:30 PM to 5:30 PM the day before yesterday. As the audience was enjoying the performance, a hoodlum named Miao Chunshan forcibly entered without buying a ticket, leading to a conflict and subsequent scuffle with ticket collector Chen Zhaoxin. Someone reported the incident to police officer Ning Zhenying from the 14th Precinct of the 4th District Public Security Bureau, who took Miao to the district office. Unexpectedly, a large group of hoodlums, some of whom were armed soldiers, arrived shortly afterward. Without asking for any explanation, they started beating people indiscriminately, causing chaos. Audience members fled in panic, and chairs, tables, teapots, and teacups flew everywhere. It is said that the theater owner, Pan Guoliang, was dragged away, and his whereabouts are unknown. Later, Pan's wife, Ms. Gu, and ticket collector Chen Zhaoxin reported the incident to the 4th District. Officer Zheng of the district conducted an inquiry. According to Ms. Gu, 42 years old, from Zhenjiang, residing at No. 36 Youyuli, Gonghe Road, her livelihood depended on the theater. Today, Miao Chunshan, accompanied by a soldier from a security force, came to watch a free show. The ticket collector argued with them, and Miao and the soldier beat him. After Miao was taken to the district office, the security force arrived, beat her husband, and dragged him away. His whereabouts are now unknown, she stated. Chen Zhaoxin, 19 years old, from the same hometown as Ms. Gu, and also residing in Youyuli, provided a similar account. Miao Chunshan claimed to be 27 years old, from Yancheng, residing at No. 28 Jiaotong Road, and working as a copper smith at the tram company. He claimed he bought a ticket to watch the show, but it was lost during the fight. His other statements were evasive. After reviewing the statements, the investigating officer noted that since Pan Guoliang was dragged away by soldiers from a security force, the specific unit and division should be investigated immediately and reported to the security force for further investigation. However, since Miao Chunshan entered without a ticket and assaulted the ticket collector, his case was transferred to the Zhabei branch of the 3rd Section of the Public Security Bureau for further action. According to theater staff, the hoodlums damaged equipment worth approximately five or six hundred yuan.

Women's National Products Year Sports Meeting

Children's Day Celebration Held

Entrance Tickets Divided into Four Groups, Primarily for Children

Invitations Extended to Cai Yuanpei and Others to Speak, with Entertainment and Gifts Provided

April 4th of this year marks the fourth Children's Day in our country. The Shanghai Women's National Products Year Sports Committee has designated this day for a grand celebration at the Hushe at the intersection of Beijing Road and Guizhou Road. Details are as follows:

Order of Events: (1) Bell Ringing to Open the Meeting, (2) All Stand at Attention, (3) Singing the Party Song, (4) Paying the Highest Respect to the Party, the National Flag, and the Portrait of Sun Yat-sen, (5) Reading Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Will, (6) Moment of Silence, (7) Chairman's Report on the Purpose of the Meeting, (8) Guest Speakers, (9) Entertainment, (10) Film Screening, (11) Adjournment. Preparations are underway throughout the venue, starting today.

Elected Officials: The officials of the meeting have been elected as follows: Madam Wu Tiecheng, Cai Zhoujun, Pan Tang Guanyu, Lin Kecong, Huang Bingpei, Madam Huang Renzhi, Liu Wang Liming, and others, totaling seven people, as the presidium; Li Manyun as the master of ceremonies; Cheng Gengnong as the recorder; Wei Zengpei, Shu Huizhen, Liu Ping Jichen, Yang Meizhen, Chen Jingrong, Chen Cuiheng as the reception; Lin Weiru as the decorator; Chen Xizhi and Xu Yiwu as the assessors of children's health; Huang Bingpei as the collector of prizes; Shen Biaohui, Zhu Dechao, Ding Guanlan as the organizers of children's amusement market and model families; Zhu Wang Huanqing as the home affairs guidance; Girl Scouts and Boy Scouts as the disciplinarians.

Four Groups Established: The association is internally divided into four groups: (1) Children's Amusement Market, (2) Model Families, (3) Home Affairs Guidance, (4) Health Competition. The China National Products Company will print and donate 2,000 entrance tickets. Each ticket is for a child. Those without children will be denied entry. At that time, children can compete in health, judged by the association, and awarded national product gifts. These gifts will be provided by various national product factories.

Speeches by Celebrities: The association has also invited Central Committee member Cai Yuanpei, Legislative Yuan member Wang Xiaoying, Executive Committee member of the Municipal Party Committee Tao Baichuan, Chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce Wang Xiaolai, Director of the Municipal Education Bureau Pan Gongzhan, President of Shanghai University Liu Zhanen, Liu Wang Lizhang of the Women's Temperance Association, as well as Huang Renzhi, Pan Yangyao, Yan Duhe, and others to speak at the event.

Entertainment and Gifts: To enhance the interest of the guests, the meeting will feature special entertainment, including (1) a play by Ms. Gu Zhen, Ms. Ye Zhenni, and Ms. Yao Biru, (2) a song and dance performance by Yucai Elementary School, (3) a song and dance drama by female employees of the China National Products Company, (4) an opera by the Yansheng Industrial Cooperative, (5) a song and dance performance by the Guanghui Orphanage, (6) a film by the China Film Education Association, (7) a song and dance performance by Ms. Qiu Tingyu of the Shanghai National Products Company, and others. Donations have been collected from national product manufacturers such as the China Chemical Industry Society, the Sanyou Industrial Society, the New Asia Pharmaceutical Factory, the Home Industry Cooperative, the Wuzhou Pharmaceutical Factory, and the Zhengyi Pharmaceutical Society for distribution to children and guests. At the same time, Mayor Wu will also produce silver commemorative badges to be distributed to children at the event. Essay Contest and Awards: Previously, the association launched an essay contest for female students to promote national products and encourage the public to use them to prevent financial leakage. After the winners were announced, an award ceremony will be held at Hushe at 1:00 PM on the 4th, with national product manufacturers donating products and cash to the winning students.

High Quality of Chinese Cement

According to the Guowen News Agency, recent news from the Shanghai construction industry indicates that Japanese cement is a major import to China. Recently, Japanese companies, noting the decline in Chinese resistance to foreign goods, have been importing large quantities of cement on Japanese ships. In addition to supplying Japanese yarn mills and other factories for expansion, they are also offering lower prices to foreign merchants. However, Shanghai Qixin and other Chinese cement factories are striving for excellence in terms of quality and color. Therefore, their sales are still quite strong, and their business is thriving. However, to prevent the mixing of Japanese goods, buyers are advised to pay attention to the brand names.

Robbers in Changan Lane Sentenced

Robbers Yu Qianxing from Ningbo and Zhu Jinsheng, a local, were sentenced for robbing the home of Ms. Lu Jiang, a local woman residing at No. 34, Lane 563, Changan Lane, Yangshupu Road, at around 5:00 AM on July 10th last year. They and their accomplices used weapons and stole several tens of yuan worth of valuables before fleeing. The case was solved on the 23rd of last month when Chinese detective Su Changsheng of the Yulin Road Police Station apprehended them. They were handed over to the First Special District Court for interrogation and trial. The court yesterday handed down the sentence in the Third Criminal Court. Yu Qianxing was sentenced to five years of imprisonment, and Zhu Jinsheng was sentenced to two years and ten months. The number of days detained before the judgment was finalized will be deducted from the sentence, with two days of detention equivalent to one day of imprisonment.

Monk Yuanying Receives Order to Take Over Jing'an Temple

Confirmed That the Temple Belongs to the Public Monastery

Decided That Yuanying Will Serve as the Abbot

According to the Guomin News Agency, the abbot of Jing'an Temple, Zhiwen, had previously been reported to have privately mortgaged temple property. The central government repeatedly ordered the municipal government to appoint impartial individuals to form a committee to investigate the temple's property. The municipal government has also announced to the public not to purchase Jing'an Temple property to avoid inconvenience. Abbot Zhiwen has long argued about the history of the temple, disputing whether it belonged to the discipleship school or the public monastery school. However, the authorities have now confirmed that the temple is indeed a public monastery. Representatives of the monastery have selected Yuanying as the new abbot of Jing'an Temple. Fearing that Abbot Zhiwen would resist the handover and secretly sell temple property, the municipal government has ordered the relevant authorities to strictly prohibit this. At the same time, the Buddhist Association has been ordered to inform the new abbot, Yuanying, to prepare to take over as soon as possible. It is reported that the new abbot Yuanying is preparing to take over.

Preparation Banquet for the Construction of the Puyi Cemetery

The Pushan Villa has been providing burials for exposed corpses, distributing coffins, and providing medicine for over twenty years. They have been dedicated to their work, leaving no stone unturned. They have collected and buried over 70,000 exposed corpses in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, contributing to public health in those areas. They have long been praised by local people. However, as their operations have expanded, their finances have become increasingly strained. The day before yesterday, they held a banquet at the Gongdelin Vegetarian Restaurant, attended by Wang Yiting, Huang Hanzhi, Yuan Ludeng, 蕢延芳, Pang Zhuqing, Zhao Wenhuan, Luo Kunxiang, Wu Zhiping, Shi Gengyin, Lao Bianbao, Chen Liangyu, Wang Junsheng, and others to discuss the construction of the Puyi Cemetery. Previously, Mr. Liu Ranqing, deeply understanding the financial difficulties of the villa, generously donated over fifty mu of farmland he owned along the Zhenda Road in Dachangzhen for the construction of the cemetery. All income generated from the land would be used to support the villa's expenses. However, while the land for the cemetery is available, funding is needed for construction. The question of how to raise these funds was brought up for discussion. After deliberation, the attendees unanimously agreed that since the cemetery meets a social need and maintains a charitable cause, serving multiple benefits at once, Yuan Ludeng and 蕢延芳 proposed a plan to invite enthusiastic philanthropists to pledge to donate certain amounts to facilitate the process. The proposal was approved by everyone, and it was also suggested to stage charity performances, inviting famous actors and opera singers to perform. There is no shortage of charitable people in Shanghai, and it is believed that ticket sales will be enthusiastic at that time.

Sheng Zhiren Discusses Labor-Capital Dispute in the Umbrella Industry

Sheng Zhiren, manager of the Zhonghua National Products Umbrella Business Office, discussed the recent labor-capital dispute in the umbrella industry, which he considered unfortunate. Although he represents the capital side, he wished to offer an impartial opinion to the public. (1) Although most capitalists are small-scale, they can abandon their individual views and unite to enthusiastically promote national product raw materials, conscientiously manufacture products, and reasonably increase selling prices, which may not be without solutions. (2) Currently, many produce shoddy goods, attempting to reduce costs by using raw materials from the East, and they treat workers poorly. Therefore, although the selling price is low, the goods are not durable, only creating competition among the capitalists themselves. (3) Workers' compensation is indeed too low. It is hoped that party and government agencies will impartially mediate the situation and prevent both sides from going to extremes. It should be stated that the business office I run always uses domestic raw materials and treats employees relatively well. Therefore, the relationship is very harmonious. This is not self-praise; there are facts to prove it.

Municipal Dental Association to Hold Second Lecture Tonight

The Shanghai Municipal Dental Association has been holding lectures since February, which have been well-received by the dental community. Professor Xu Junmin of the Shanghai Dental College will be the speaker, and the topic will be "Accidental Complications Encountered in Dental Clinical Practice and Their Treatment." Deng Cigan, Involved in Roulette Gambling Den Case, Remains at Large

Deng Has Fled to Hong Kong, Case Not Yet Heard

The Russian Yao Kesutu, formerly pretending to be a Brazilian national, leased a large building from the British company Taili Yangxing on Avenue Edward VII to open a roulette gambling den. The General Inspectorate learned of this and sent Chinese and foreign detectives to arrest the Russian, who was then handed over to the First Special District Court for trial. He was found guilty and sentenced to two years of imprisonment and a fine of three thousand yuan. It is now known that a Cantonese man named Deng Cigan was also involved with the Russian. However, Deng fled when the gambling den was raided. The police have filed a public prosecution against Deng. The First Special Court recently issued a summons for trial, but Deng did not surrender. Wu Saitai, a lawyer, appeared in court and claimed that Deng had gone to Hong Kong, requesting a postponement. Therefore, the case was not heard. The judge approved a postponement for the trial.

Contributions of the China Child Welfare Association

"Parents' Studies" Has Been Published

The China Child Welfare Association, as the promoter of Children's Day in China, has specially published the book "Parents' Studies" (Modern Parents' Series) during this year's nationwide celebration of Children's Day, for the use of those who promote or study parental education throughout China. This is a memorable event. It is reported that the book was written by Professor Ailide, a professor of child psychology at St. Xingnaide University in the United States. It provides detailed and insightful discussions and insights into various issues faced by modern parents and has long been renowned in Europe and the United States, widely read and memorized, and is a valuable resource for promoting parental education. Chinese child education expert Mr. Chen Heqin praised the book as (1) having a scientific basis, (2) having revolutionary suggestions, (3) having appropriate and rich examples. Its value can be seen. The entire book is divided into sixteen chapters, written in a lively and interesting style. During this nationwide celebration of Children's Day and promotion of children's well-being, all parents, those preparing to become parents, and all school teachers should read a copy. The actual price per copy is six jiao.

Six Russians Arrested for Smoking Heroin

Lang Bole, a Western detective from the Second Investigation Group of the French Police, recently discovered that someone was stuffing the drug heroin into cigarettes at No. 784 Avenue Joffre, exclusively for lower-class Russians to smoke for pleasure, in violation of the ban. At 3:00 PM the day before yesterday, he led Russian detectives to search the address. They found six Russians, Cheernastinsky, Wudiyaguf, Xinaniguf, Weituoliaifu, Zhilinggisky, and Shaliuquanna, sitting in a room smoking these cigarettes. They were all arrested, and several heroin cigarettes were confiscated. They were taken to the police station to await trial.

Laborer Dies from Crushed Spine

Liu A'san, a 34-year-old laborer from Jiangbei, was employed at the Yan Zhenhe bridal shop in Huacao Xiaoyangbang, West Shanghai. He was usually very diligent in his duties. The day before yesterday afternoon, Liu was making woodenware in the shop and went to the area where wood was piled by the river to carry a large piece of wood on his shoulder. Unexpectedly, he was too weak to bear the weight and was pressed down. The wood crushed his spine, causing him to fall to the ground and vomit blood, dying instantly. His fellow laborers were shocked and immediately tried to rescue him, but they were unable to do anything. The incident was discovered by the First Precinct of the Sixth District. In addition to sending police to summon the shop owner for investigation, the head of the 37th Bao, 5th Tu, Chen Yuetang, was ordered to report the case to the local court for verification. In the afternoon, Prosecutor Yang and others arrived at the scene to verify the cause of death. It was confirmed that the death was caused by crushing. The shop was instructed to handle the funeral arrangements, pending further investigation.

News on the Zhang Zhiyun Case Yesterday

Zhang Zhiyun, who was once elected as the first "Movie Queen," filed a criminal complaint against Zhou Xiaobo, accusing him of violating their cohabitation agreement. She retained lawyer Dan Yuhua to prosecute Zhou for offenses against public morals. The First Special District Court opened the trial twice, but neither party appeared. Zhang Zhiyun even submitted a petition to the court, denying that she had accused Zhou and requesting a thorough investigation. The matter is so confusing that outsiders cannot understand the truth, and the court is almost lost in a fog. They will investigate thoroughly. It was learned from a certain source that Zhang Zhiyun personally visited the court on the afternoon of the 30th of last month. However, the trial had already concluded when she arrived, so Zhang did not go to the Eighth Tribunal and returned home. Afterwards, Zhang told people that she would definitely surrender at the next hearing, explain the entire process of the dispute with Zhou, and dispel all kinds of doubts. If so, the case may move from a situation of confusion to one of clarity.

Jiangsu Farmers Bank to Relieve the Rural Economy of Northern Jiangsu

Expanding the Northern Jiangsu Farmers Bank

Promoting Cooperative Organizations

According to the Central News Agency, the Jiangsu Provincial Farmers Bank, as the sole institution for relieving rural finance in the province, has been established for five years. Over the years, its business has progressed. Since the reorganization of the bank in January of this year, its operations have developed rapidly, with many reforms, and its business has shown a rapid leap forward compared to before. At a time when the rural economy is bankrupt, the bank is becoming more and more valued. The reporter, based on investigations from various aspects, now selects and records the recent handling of the bank as follows:

In the past years, it has been found that the bank's capital is 2.6 million yuan, and there are already 24 branches.

Development Status According to the bank's report, as of March 15th this year, all loans, deposits, and collections have made significant progress. The savings and deposit items alone increased by more than 900,000 yuan in two and a half months, which is an unprecedented phenomenon in the bank's history.

Recruiting Talents The Farmers Bank is a bank of a special nature, and its operating methods and internal affairs are not

Calculating Talents Without specialized talent, it is not enough to be competent. The bank's general manager, Mr. Zhao Dihua, was originally a financial and accounting expert, formerly the chief accountant of the National Government's Accounting Office and the deputy director of the Accounting Bureau, and a professor of accounting at various universities for many years. This time, in charge of the Farmers Bank, in addition to seeking to expand branches externally, expand business, and promote cooperative undertakings, he also pays attention to the improvement of internal work systems and the recruitment of specialized talents. Those who are recruited are mostly in their original positions and are being extended an invitation through the bank's efforts. Recently, the bank urgently needs to improve the accounting system, and the existing accounting talent is insufficient to allocate, so it used examination methods to select specialized talent.

Promoting Agriculture Because the bank feels that its business center is in loans and organized agricultural production cooperatives, but Jiangsu's cooperatives often only have a nominal reputation and rarely have practical effects. It has now sent many experts to various places to actively reorganize and promote various cooperatives so that they can also engage in production, transportation, sales, purchasing, utilization, and other businesses, so as to actually promote agricultural production.

Relieving the Northern To expand the practical effect of rescuing farmers (especially farmers in Northern Jiangsu)

Jiangsu Countryside, the bank is actively and tirelessly progressing in the establishment of branches. In addition to the Yixing branch, which will soon open, the Jinshan sub-branch is currently in preparation, and the Jintan business office has been expanded into a branch. It is said that in the future, it will focus its efforts on the promotion of branches in Northern Jiangsu, such as Qingpu, Suqian, Suining, and Donghai. The bank is planning separately to set up branches immediately. Recently, it was also heard that the bank has joined the Construction Department and the Education Department to convene a discussion meeting on the unified cooperative business in Northern Jiangsu, in order to actually relieve the rural economy in Northern Jiangsu.

Lu Xungong's Coffin Postponed for Shipment to Shanghai for Burial

Mr. Lu Xungong, a pioneer of the Chinese revolution, passed away due to heart disease at his residence in Beiping on June 12th last year. At that time, because the Japanese invaders were in North China, and Peiping and Tianjin were in imminent danger, his family, in order to admire the late person's long-cherished ambition of worrying about the country and forgetting personal matters, did not announce the news to relatives and friends, so few people outside knew about it. Now his family has decided to receive the post in Peiping on March 29th, and originally planned to transport the coffin to Shanghai on March 31st and bury it on April 3rd. Now, due to circumstances, it has been changed to April 2nd, to transport the coffin from Peiping to Shanghai, and it will be shipped from the North Station at 1:00 pm on April 3rd, and buried in the Public Works Department Cemetery on Hongqiao Road at 3:00 pm.

Self-accusation Deemed Unsuitable, Public Prosecution Filed Instead, Resulting in the Acquittal of the Defendants

Wu Suzhen, a woman from Changzhou, is 33 years old this year. She was already married and had a family in her hometown. She came to Shanghai in October of last year and met Zhang Huafu from Nanjing, Shen Meiying, a woman from Wuxi, and Wang Changfa, who is now at large. The three of them invited her to the Empire Theater in the French Concession to watch a movie. It happened that Chen Jinding, the owner of a flower shop at No. 45 Jin Shenfu Road in the French Concession (45 years old this year), was also watching the movie in the theater. After the show, because Chen was acquainted with Zhang and others, he invited Wu Suzhen, Zhang, and others to open a room at the Tiansheng Hotel in Baxianqiao to have some refreshments. Zhang, Shen, and Wang told Wu that Chen's wife had passed away and he urgently needed to remarry, using their eloquent tongues to broker the match. Suzhen was temporarily bewitched and became drunk from the wine. That night, she was raped by Chen, and her heart was swayed, and she was willing to marry Chen. After another round of persuasion from Zhang and others, Suzhen returned to her hometown to divorce her former husband. At the same time, on the 28th of that month, she and Chen held a wedding ceremony at the Hexinglou restaurant on Aiduya Road and Chengdu Road. After inviting guests, Suzhen lived at Chen's place. A few days later, she accompanied Chen back to his home in Dachang, and saw that Chen's wife was alive and well, and had a son and a daughter. Suzhen was greatly shocked, and argued with Chen to no avail, and immediately returned to Shanghai and went back to Changzhou, and told her mother, Wu Zhang, who came to Shanghai together. Zhang, as the legal representative, and Suzhen jointly hired a lawyer to file a complaint with the Second Special District Court, accusing Chen Jinding, Zhang Huafu, Shen Meiying, and others of colluding to commit bigamy, requesting an investigation and prosecution, and attaching a civil suit to recover losses. The court summoned them based on the complaint. The details have been recorded in this newspaper last year. Subsequently, after trial, it was found that Wu Suzhen had gone through a marriage ceremony with Chen Jinding and was a spouse, which was not in accordance with the self-accusation procedure, so the self-accusation was ruled inadmissible. Wu Suzhen was unwilling to accept this, and submitted marriage certificates, gift books, invitation cards, and other evidence, and reported to the French police, requesting the initiation of a public prosecution according to law. The police chief immediately sent Detective Qian Yumin to arrest Chen Jinding, Zhang Huafu, Shen Meiying, and others. Wang Changfa was at large and could not be arrested. Then the police transferred Chen and the others to the Second Special District Court, and initiated a public prosecution on charges of bigamy. The details were also briefly recorded in the previous newspaper. During the trial, Chen Jinding confessed that he and the plaintiff Wu Suzhen had a relationship, but he did not marry her as a concubine. All the marriage certificates, etc., were written by Suzhen's brother. I am illiterate and do not know about this plan of framing me, and I was really fooled. Zhang Huafu, Shen Meiying, and others also denied being matchmakers, only introducing them to have an affair. After Judge Tu Shenjie opened court several times to summon witnesses, the result of the trial was that the evidence and reasons presented by the plaintiff were insufficient, and the defendants were acquitted the day before yesterday. During the appeal period, the defendants were all released on bail pending further instruction.

Ten Thousand People Compete to See the Big Wax Candles

Yangjiazhai Supported About 400 Jin

The Pengchang Temple in the east end of Hongqiao Town in western Shanghai, initiated by the villagers, held a three-day victory meeting from March 31st to April 2nd to erect tower lamp poles. There were a total of 42 tower lamp poles erected on the open space of the temple fair. At about 6:00 pm in the evening, each lamp pole was lit, the red candles were shining brightly, which was quite spectacular. At the same time, the sound of firecrackers was deafening, and the large wax candles lit in front of the gods in the temple were no less than two hundred pairs. Among them, the ones supported by Yangjiazhai were the largest, about 400 jin. Therefore, the red men and women who came to watch from the four villages were extremely crowded, almost like on Shanyin Road, which was a grand occasion unprecedented.

Impersonating A Police Officer, Search of the Red Pill Dealer Exposed

Hu Yaohua Arrested at the Door

Zhang Jude's firewood and charcoal store on Xiaojiuhua Road in Nanshi also operates a rice and grain business, specializing in wholesale business in this port, which is very large. It has been open for more than ten years. Chen Meisheng, the manager, was closing the shop at about 6:00 pm the other day when four plainclothes men suddenly came to the store and claimed, "We are sent by the Public Security Bureau. Someone reported to the bureau that there are privately hidden red pills and contraband items here. The bureau sent us to search." They presented a search warrant for inspection. The store claimed that there were no contraband items hidden and, seeing that there was a search warrant from the bureau, allowed the search. After about two hours, they found nothing and left. The store felt aggrieved for being framed and immediately reported to the Firewood and Charcoal Guild, and sent a letter to the Municipal Public Security Bureau and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, requesting a thorough investigation of the person who framed them and to punish them. The Municipal Public Security Bureau specially sent Inspector Li to the store the other day to investigate, saying that the Public Security Bureau had not sent anyone to search, which was obviously someone impersonating them to seek extortion. The bureau is now investigating and punishing them. Suddenly, the day before yesterday afternoon, one of the people who searched the store passed by the door and was seen by a friend of the store, who stepped forward and arrested him, and called the police to detain him at the first branch of the first district. When questioned, he said his name was Hu Yaohua, and he lived in Dadongmen. He used to work at the Public Security Bureau. He confessed to searching the store and was immediately sent to the Public Security Bureau for punishment.

Summary of Bank Inspection Reports

The Central Bank's 192nd Inspection Report on Issuance Preparation states that, in accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, this committee is responsible for inspecting the gold reserves for the issuance of convertible notes of this bank. The 192nd inspection was held at the Issuance Bureau of this bank on March 31, 1934. The results of the inspection are hereby announced as follows: (A) The total amount of convertible notes issued is 68,368,222 silver dollars, including 61,920,890 silver dollar notes and 6,447,332 fractional currency notes. The total amount of gold reserves for convertible notes is 68,368,222 silver dollars, including 55,312,222 silver dollars in cash reserves. This cash reserve includes 51,717,427 yuan deposited in the issuance vault of this bank, 1,796,872 yuan deposited in branches in various ports, and 1,797,923 yuan deposited in commerce. The guaranteed reserve is equivalent to 13,056,000 silver dollars. (B) The total amount of customs gold convertible notes issued is 373,324.70 yuan. The total amount of gold reserves for customs gold convertible notes is 373,324.70 yuan. This reserve includes 7,351 taels, 9 qian, and 5 fen of standard gold, which is equivalent to 373,324.70 yuan in customs gold at the fixed price of 50779. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank's Convertible Note Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guaranteed reserve is 40%. The result of this inspection is that the cash exceeds 60% and the guarantee is less than 40%, which is in compliance with the regulations. This report is hereby made. April 2, 1934, Supervisory Committee of the Central Bank, Chairman Li Fuxun, Supervisors Xie Mingxun, Bei Songsun, Zhai Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jilong.

China General Chamber of Commerce Bank's Issuance Preparation Inspection Report states that the China General Chamber of Commerce Bank's issuance of convertible notes and gold reserves for March 1934 have now been inspected by supervisors Fu Qilin, He Shaoyin, and Xie Jishan, together with accountant Xu Yongzuo, on April 2. The results of the inspection are listed as follows: The total amount of convertible notes issued is 17,254,900 yuan. The total amount of gold reserves is 17,254,900 yuan, including 12,686,400 yuan in cash reserves, more than 60%, and 4,568,500 yuan in guaranteed reserves, less than 40%, which is in compliance with the issuance regulations.

Social Novel (Dark Paradise) Publication The Society's full-length novel (Dark Paradise) is the latest carefully crafted masterpiece by the famous novelist Cheng Zhanlu. The entire book scolds the treachery of people's hearts and the warmth and coldness of the world, and exposes the evils of the city and the darkness of society. It can be said to be profound and meticulous, with a tortuous structure, tense and enthusiastic, and a humorous and thought-provoking writing style. Weather Report

Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 pm yesterday stated that the wind direction and weather conditions in northeastern China and Shandong are uncertain due to a low pressure passing through Mongolia and moving towards the southeast east. The Yangtze River basin and this area are cloudy with light fog, and the wind is unstable. The coastal area south of Ma'anshan Island is cloudy with fog or mist and northeasterly winds. Also, within 24 hours before 3:00 pm yesterday, the temperature in this port was 56.3 degrees at the highest and 36.1 degrees at the lowest. On the same day last year, the temperature was 58.6 degrees at the highest and 44.6 degrees at the lowest.

Small Preface A reader from this port came to visit our Club. As soon as we met, we asked him for criticisms of the work of reading guidance. He said: "A criticism is not good, but how can the (Reading Q&A) be made interesting for ordinary shop assistants and apprentices to read?" So we asked him, "How many people are there in your shop? How many people are happy to read (Reading Q&A)?" He laughed and said, "There are more than 160 people in the shop, including senior staff, and only 30 to 40 people like to read (Reading Q&A). And among these 30 to 40 people, only seven or eight people really understand it!" After hearing this, we were both happy that our work could win the sympathy of a quarter of the 160 people, and naturally fearful and ashamed. It turned out that our work was so impractical. This is a clear criticism of our work, and it is extremely fair. A certain gentleman's trainee, who himself cannot fully understand everything discussed in (Reading Q&A), and the few words he said, we consider them extremely valuable. We really need to hear the opinions of our basic readers themselves. Therefore, we have no choice but to make the following efforts for the (Reading Q&A) in the future: First, for ourselves: (1) In terms of writing expression, we will try as much as possible to be popular so that it is not difficult to read, (2) We will try to avoid theoretical discussions that are too far away from general life, (3) We will use more practical examples to explain theories and talk less about principles. Second, for readers, we also have the following hopes: (1) (Reading Q&A) is not necessarily that we talk too deeply, but the attitude of (Reading Q&A) is more serious than that of general tabloids. Its content is theoretical exploration. We hope that people who are already interested in (Reading Q&A) will often entice those who are still infatuated with low-level interest reading materials to come and see (Reading Q&A.) (2) For (new nouns), (terms), and (theories themselves), I hope readers will try their best to absorb, learn hard, and not be too afraid of difficulties or too conservative. These (new nouns) and (terms) are all generated in modern daily life. If we want to be modern people, we really have no way to avoid using them, and we must be able to understand these things to read modern newspapers and books. (3) As for the content, we cannot lower it to cater to the level of low-level interests. We ask the readers to (catch up) and not (give up) if they cannot catch up. At the same time, we also hope that readers can specifically point out the errors in (Reading Q&A).

Weekly Information (1) Ten reading comrades participated this week, including one female comrade. (2) Received 67 letters for discussion and replied to 42 letters. (3) Received ten letters requesting the organization of reading groups and six letters transferred by the postal lending department requesting the library to publish a regular publication. Five people came to talk. (4) This department decided: A Conduct a survey of readers' reading life for three months since the commencement of the reading guidance. The survey form will be sent out before the 10th. B For readers of this newspaper from other ports who have participated in the Reading Guidance Department for one month, if they are really interested in research and continue to communicate and discuss, and submit reading reports to this department, this department can introduce the postal lending department of this library to enjoy the right to borrow books, but the procedures will be determined separately. C All questions that are not within the scope of the department's answers, such as requests to introduce occupations, inquiries about school secrets, introductions to Western books and newspapers, suggestions to this newspaper, and questions that are too specialized (such as inquiries about the installation of spinning machines and the breeding of goldfish), will not be answered in the future. D (Reading Q&A) will be published as usual during the spring break.

Mailbox (1) To readers of this department: (1) Please fill out the Reading Life Survey Form of this department for three months before April 15 and send it to the library. If you have not communicated with this department for a long time, please also explain the reason for not communicating for a long time. Those who do not send the reply letter to the library before the 30th will be deemed to have voluntarily withdrawn from this department, and the registration will be cancelled immediately. (2) You can use (1), (2), (3), etc. to mark the questions raised in the letter, and do not use polite words at all; for questions of different nature, please raise them twice. (3) Please do not raise questions that are too empty and have no content. It is best to raise them specifically based on a certain book or a certain newspaper. (2) To readers of Shen Bao: (1) All communications between readers of Shen Bao and this department are valid only if they have a communication stamp (that is, the one attached to the title of (Reading Q&A) every day); those without stamps will not be answered. (2) Please pay attention to the second and third regulations of (To readers of this department) when asking questions. (3) Please conduct a survey of the number of people around you who read (Reading Q&A) and their opinions on (Reading Q&A).

Chun Qiu

People from Jiangbei

— Hua Ling

I am not very clear about the situation elsewhere. In Shanghai, no matter who it is, when (Jiangbei people) are mentioned, they will pull down the corners of their mouths and sink their eyes, (humph)ing in their noses, expressing a hundred and twenty points of disdain.

Indeed, the position of (Jiangbei people) in Shanghai is like that of (Chinese) in the eyes of Europeans and Americans, a semi-civilized nation.

In Shanghai, in addition to (foreigners), (Ningbo people), (Guangdong people), and (Jiangbei people) stand as a tripod, supporting the market of Greater Shanghai. However, (Jiangbei people) are ultimately not as popular as (Ningbo people) and (Guangdong people). It is said that most (Jiangbei people) are engaged in humble occupations and rarely have (Kang Bai Du)-style high-class Chinese. This is the first level. The second level is that (Jiangbei people) lack mutual assistance and unity, and do not seek revenge when wronged. Another reason is that during the Battle of Shanghai, there was a traitor headquarters in Zhabei: the (Jiangbei Headquarters).

Regarding the first level, I think the thinking is already outdated. (Jiangbei people) exchange labor for bread, I ask, what are they ashamed of to heaven or to earth? The second level is indeed very meaningful, and it is precisely this that plagues the common disease of the (Chinese). As for the last level, it is simply an insult to the entire (Jiangbei people), because how could the former senior officials of the (Jiangbei Headquarters) be (Jiangbei people)?

Although the author grew up in Jiangnan, she lived in Jiangbei for more than ten years, so she is extremely aware that (Jiangbei people) are more accustomed to diligence and hard work than people in any other place, and are honest and loyal in nature. And I feel extremely unfair about the position of (Jiangbei people) in Shanghai. I hope that in the near future, in Shanghai, (Jiangbei people) will spontaneously rise up to establish (Jiangbei Bank), (Jiangbei Hotel), (Jiangbei University), and (Jiangbei Dance Hall). Then build a (Jiangbei Building) and organize a (Jiangbei Fellow Association), showing the (Jiangbei people)'s face all at once.

Believe it or not?

— Shao

Starting from the last column of a thirteen-column abacus, push the beads up one by one, carrying one for every ten. When will it be possible to fill these beads? Eating, going out, and sleeping – the three major events are not counted; it will take until the thirty-first century!

If everyone continuously has four sons and none of them die young (they can only die after they have finished having children), in two hundred years, a small city of children can be created, with a total population of 262,144 children. (Assuming childbearing starts at age twenty-two.)

Foreigners

— Wofo

The tram was running along the tracks like clouds, and the seats on both sides of the car were crowded. The ticket seller seemed to be still free, looking at the few tickets folded up on his ticket tray for a while, and then shifting his gaze from horizontal to vertical, shooting it outside the window. A few passengers were also voluntarily paying attention for the ticket seller (Here! A foreigner!) A young passenger shouted this very quickly. Before the tram arrived at X station, a foreigner did jump on the tram, but the ticket seller’s few folded tickets had disappeared. While the foreigner was checking the tickets one by one, a tense atmosphere appeared in the quiet air, and the ticket seller's face was occasionally cast with glances.

(Here! A foreigner!) A vendor who was the first to shoulder his orange load and hurried into the alley to hide gave a warning to the other vendors as he got up. Their [the vendors'] senses are truly sharp. In the blink of an eye, the baskets, bamboo baskets, trays... had all disappeared, and only a few heads were sticking out from the nearby alleys. (He's gone, the foreigner!) Under the cheering of most people [vendors], the baskets, loads, bamboo baskets, trays... reappeared, connecting seamlessly.

Mr. X was hosting a dinner party at his house. After drinking, in addition to setting up a mahjong table, there was also a pai gow table. Everyone was smiling as they gambled, and there were also onlookers. (Here! A foreigner!) Although everyone didn't know where the shout came from, they hurriedly pushed the pai gow under the table without thinking or hesitating, and people also scurried aimlessly into several pigeonhole-like rooms. After a while of silence, everyone suddenly burst out laughing, with scolding mixed in the laughter. It turned out that it was a child from the neighbor's house who had lied.

(Here! A foreigner!) You can often hear this shout when you walk on the road, but I don't know who taught him [the foreigner] to come??

Common sense

Ten Commandments of Smoking

— Chu Yu

Smoking is originally harmful to the brain and stomach, but it also has the effect of avoiding plague and eliminating filth. However, if an addict suddenly quits, it is easy to contract a virus. Now, to prevent nicotine poisoning, there are ten key points that smokers should pay close attention to.

1. Dry tobacco, moldy tobacco, and damp, old tobacco. Because nicotine is easily liberated, it is easy to be poisoned when smoking.

2. Once a cigarette is smoked halfway and the flame goes out, do not smoke it again. If you want to smoke it, finish it, or discard it. Because when a cigarette is smoked halfway and goes out, nicotine condenses in the ashes, and this nicotine poison is very potent.

3. When lighting a cigarette, never inhale the green smoke emitted from matches. Whenever a match is struck and lit, do not rush to light the cigarette, lest phosphorus poison enter the mouth.

4. When inhaling smoke, be sure to keep your mouth closed and exhale through your nostrils, because smoke entering the nose is most likely to damage the brain.

5. Cigar tobacco has the most nicotine, so it should be avoided. If you are heavily addicted to tobacco, it should be smoked in a long pipe for safety.

6. Smoking after eating or on an empty stomach is not appropriate; smoking while drinking is strictly forbidden.

7. Do not smoke when angry or unhappy, because your mind, whether excited or depressed, is easily poisoned by nicotine.

8. When smoking various cigarettes, a long cigarette holder should be used so that nicotine accumulates in the cigarette holder and is not easily inhaled directly. See below for details on other medicines to prevent nicotine poisoning.

9. Smoke no more than five cigarettes a day; more is harmful. Your body should be checked annually for nicotine poisoning.

10. When smoking indoors, air should be circulated; do not close windows tightly, lest smoke fill the air.

Nicotine Poisoning

— Chu Yu

We smokers should know the poisonous quality of nicotine in various tobaccos. However, the amount of nicotine varies depending on the types produced in each country. Now, the poisonous qualities contained in the tobaccos shipped to China from various countries are listed as follows: Egyptian cigarettes contain 2.2 to 1.5 percent; British, French, and American tobacco leaves contain 2.0 to 3.5 percent; Virginia cigars contain 3.5 percent; Brittany tobacco leaves contain 2 percent; Jamaican tobacco leaves contain 1.2 percent; Borldini Negro tobacco leaves contain 1.2 percent; Swiss Berisha tobacco leaves contain 2 to 4 percent; Tuscan cigarettes contain 2 to 4 percent; Oriental tobacco leaves contain 0.8 to 1.2 percent; French cigarettes contain 2 to 3.5 percent; British and American cigarettes contain 1.1 to 2.9 percent. The tobacco leaves produced in the Crimean Peninsula have the highest nicotine content, and the Xinchang tobacco leaves in Zhejiang, China, have the least nicotine content. The amount of nicotine can be determined by the color of the tobacco leaves; light-colored ones have more, and dark-colored ones have less. Nicotine is colorless and odorless; if placed in the air, it turns brown. The lethal dose for nicotine poisoning is 0.03 to 0.06 grams, which is the amount contained in a large tobacco leaf and five cigars. However, people who are addicted to it can tolerate five or six times that amount. If the nicotine in tobacco is reduced by 0.1 percent, the tobacco loses its original flavor, because most of the aroma in tobacco is formed by nicotine. However, not all aromas are nicotine; for example, Egyptian cigarettes have a rich aroma but a very low nicotine content. The acute symptoms of nicotine poisoning include a pale face, cold sweats, salivation, vomiting, nausea, vomiting, diarrhea, low blood pressure, collapse, and weakness. However, advocates of nicotine say that nicotine can stimulate the sympathetic nervous system and promote the secretion of adrenaline from the adrenal glands, which can increase blood sugar and blood pressure. As for the prevention of nicotine poisoning, you can take some tannic acid or use 0.3 percent ammonium chloride or ammonium ferric citrate and instill it into the pipe and inhale, or you can soak cotton with the above-mentioned medicines and plug it into the mouthpiece, which can also eliminate nicotine poisoning.

Royal Incense飘渺录 [A Faint Record of Royal Incense]

— Qin Shoujuan

Introduction to the original author: Qing Princess Der Ling

She and Mr. T. White once had a son, who unfortunately died of illness last spring. Needless to say, our abandoned old woman’s heart suffered an even deeper wound. So, when she submitted this work for publication, she specifically wrote a very painful sentence on the first page, which is In Loving Memory of my son Thaddens Raymond White (In memory of my beloved deceased son Thaddeus Raymond White).

Now, she lives alone in New York, relying solely on the income from selling articles to make a living. But it is said that she has no intention of returning home. This is a brief biography of the original author, Princess Der Ling.

Didn't I say above that they have a total of five siblings, and the four of them have already passed away? The second and fifth also enjoyed a great reputation. Moreover, when the translator was engaged in translation this time, both of them gave me very grateful guidance through the introduction of my friend Tang Yunfan. Here I can also introduce them to the reader. In this book, they are also a very important part. Xun Ling is currently sixty years old and is the second brother of the original author. He is the one who inherited his father's title. He was very favored when Empress Dowager Cixi was in power. At the same time, he is also a senior photographer with great research on photography. None of the photos taken of Cixi in her life were not taken by him. He is currently living a very comfortable life as a retired gentleman in Beiping.

Rong Ling, also known as Princess Shanshou (given by Cixi, referring to Longevity Mountain), is the biological sister of the original author, ranked fifth. She is currently the wife of General Tang Baochao and is considered a very prominent figure in Beiping social circles. She also served as a lady-in-waiting to Empress Dowager Cixi in the inner court, and later wrote a book in English called (Xiang Fei), which is still popular and praised by many people in Europe and America.

Because of the guidance of the two of them, the translator was able to translate it without missing a word, which is really gratifying. However, the crudeness of the translation still cannot be concealed. I am ashamed, I am ashamed! (II)

Northeast Four Company Commander

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twenty-sixth

Generously revealing his heart to serve the country, forgetting his family; sadly facing the jade mirror, sighing for my sweetheart.

This shout startled Gui Zhi, who quickly took out a handkerchief to wipe her tears, replying, "Nothing? The raindrops are too noisy to sleep, so I thought I'd find something to do, but I haven't started yet." Jiang Shi had already entered the hall and was pushing the bedroom door with her hand, saying, "Open it, I have something to say to you." Gui Zhi originally didn't want to open the door, but since her mother had secretly come to visit, it must be for a purpose. If she didn't let her in, she would become even more suspicious. So, she first turned up the flame of the kerosene lamp a bit higher, then opened the door and let Jiang Shi in. Jiang Shi entered the room and first looked up at Gui Zhi's face, saying, "Child, why are you crying?" Gui Zhi forced a smile and said, "I'm not crying!" Jiang Shi said, "How can you say you're not crying? I've been watching outside the window for a long time." Gui Zhi knew that she couldn't deny it, so she sighed and said, "I was thinking about it here. It's so cold here now. I was thinking that it must be even colder outside the pass. Since Ziqiang left, he sent a letter on the day he arrived, but now I don't know if he's still at Xifengkou." Jiang Shi said, "You're overthinking it. If he's fine, why would he keep writing to you? If he had changed his location, wouldn't he have sent a letter home?" Gui Zhi didn't say anything, but picked up the photo on the table and hung it back on the wall. But she used one index finger to wipe away all the tears that had dripped on the photo. Jiang Shi stood next to her and pressed her arm with her hand, whispering, "Child, you're a smart person, how can you be so pessimistic? Your father-in-law is thinking about you day and night. If you do this, aren't you just adding to the old man's worries?" (353)

Jiangda Basketball Concludes

Six Wins in Six Games, Victory Over Daxia Yesterday

Fudan University Wins Championship

Almost Defeated by Daxia Yesterday

Daxia Faces Challenge with Only Four Players in the End

Result: 34 to 22

The Fudan University basketball team won every game in this Jiangda Basketball Championship. Yesterday afternoon, they played their final game against Daxia at the Daxia court. The Daxia athletes performed exceptionally well and showed great strength. Although Fudan was strong, they were unfamiliar with the court, which made them helpless and almost lost. In the first half, Daxia took the lead with 12 to 10. In the second half, Daxia continued to lead. Later, three Daxia players, Jing Jianling, Li Desheng, and Ren Jiexing, successively committed four fouls and had to leave the court. Because there were no replacements, they had to face the challenge with only four players. Fudan took the opportunity to rise and finally reversed the defeat with 34 to 22, winning this championship.

Tense Situation, Fudan Falls Behind

At the beginning of the game, both sides had tight defenses, and no points were scored for a long time. Suddenly, Fudan gained momentum and took the lead with three points. Daxia refused to be outdone, and Chen Zhaoqiu scored two shots, surpassing them with four to three. The Daxia athletes fought more and more vigorously, leading all the way. Fudan tried to make a comeback and once tied the score at eight to nine. In this tense situation, Chen Zhaoqiu made two more excellent shots. The first half ended with Daxia leading with 12 to 10.

Daxia Suffers a Miserable Defeat Facing Challenge with Four Players

As the second half began, Fudan worked harder and competed fiercely. The score went back and forth repeatedly. Before long, with the efforts of Qiu Guangxie, Fudan caught up with 14 to 13. However, Daxia quickly added two goals, making it 17 to 14. Daxia defender Li Longsheng committed four fouls and had to leave the court. Fudan scored another goal, making it 20 to 16. Then, Zhang Jinxiang penetrated under the basket, and Zhong Enling also committed four fouls. Zhang made three points with one shot, making it 20 to 19. When Qiu Guangxie scored two free throws, Fudan finally surpassed them with 21 to 20. At this time, Ren Jiexing also had to leave the court. Daxia faced the challenge with four players, outnumbered and inevitably defeated. The final score was 34 to 22.
